# CDiscourse — Current Status
<!-- Latest implementer card: QOL-042 (Linked prior argument reference as context). Full suite is 8521 tests / 303 suites. -->

## QOL-042 — Linked prior argument reference as context (Epic — Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review — lets a new argument room **reference an earlier settled room** as context. The reference is a one-directional, immutable **link record** between two rooms (`public.argument_room_links`): the new room surfaces a context **chip** carrying the prior room's title; a private prior room's *content* opens only for a user authorized on the original room (an unauthorized viewer sees the **title only** — never body, nodes, or evidence); the locked prior room is **never re-opened or mutated** by the link. **One new append-only migration** (write-only — the operator applies it post-merge); **no Edge Function** — RLS + two BEFORE triggers fully enforce the link rules. No service-role, no direct insert into `public.arguments`, no `submit-argument` change, no new dependency, no Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no `.env` touched. Issue #211.

- **What it ships — migration (write-only):** `supabase/migrations/20260521000010_qol042_argument_room_links.sql` — the `argument_room_links` table (`source_debate_id` → CASCADE, `target_debate_id` → RESTRICT, `created_by` → `public.profiles`, `target_title_snapshot text ≤200` for the title-only state, `note text ≤280`, `is_removed` soft-remove, `no_self_link` + `one_link_per_pair` constraints), RLS enabled with **exactly four §7 policies** (SELECT gated on source-room visibility; INSERT by a source-room participant as `created_by = auth.uid()`; UPDATE soft-remove by the link author or an admin) and **no DELETE policy**, two partial indexes on active rows (source + target), and two BEFORE triggers — `link_target_must_be_locked` (the target must be a settled `locked` room the inserting user can read) and `link_columns_immutable` (only `is_removed` may change after insert).
- **What it ships — pure models + API + UI:** New `src/features/arguments/crossRoom/` module — `linkedPriorArgumentModel.ts` (`ArgumentRoomLink`, `LinkAccessState` `authorized` / `title_only` / `unavailable`, `buildLinkedPriorArgumentChip` producing the chip's three view states, `canCreateLink` true only for a `locked` target, `buildLinkedTangentContext` a pure formatter that keeps `archived_or_resolved` tangent nodes — degrading to all tangent nodes when LIFE-001 stage data is absent, design §14 Q4); `linkedPriorArgumentCopy.ts` (every user-facing string, doctrine-ban-list held); `argumentRoomLinksApi.ts` (caller-scoped wrappers — `listLinksForRoom`, `createArgumentRoomLink` with idempotent-duplicate handling, `removeArgumentRoomLink` soft-remove, `loadPriorRoomContext` deriving `LinkAccessState` from the RLS outcome); `LinkedPriorArgumentChipRow.tsx` (the timeline context-chip row — a disabled "Open prior argument" action shows a visible reason + `accessibilityState` disabled). `ArgumentTimelineMap.tsx` gains an additive optional `linkedPriorChips` prop rendering the chip row in the timeline header above the rail; `oneBox/boxModel.ts` gains an additive optional `linkedPriorRoomId` on the `Draft` buffer (root_claim setup); `oneBox/inspectPopoutModel.ts` gains the additive `buildInspectLinkedPriorSection` ("From the linked prior argument" — visible only when the chip is authorized; the fixed seven-section set is untouched). `src/lib/types.ts` re-exports `ArgumentRoomLink` as a cross-feature domain type.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the link is **context, never a verdict** — no truth field, no score, no relationship-type enum; the chip never says the prior argument "won", "proved", or "was correct". The move counts on the chip are **activity** facts, never standing. The access check is **RLS-enforced server-side** — a `title_only` viewer's prior-room body / nodes are gated by the existing `debates` / `arguments` RLS; the model only *renders* the `LinkAccessState` the API client derived. **Minimal disclosure** — the single denormalized field is the prior room's *title* (≤200 chars); no body, node text, evidence, or participant identity is ever copied onto the link. The locked prior room's immutability is **structurally enforced** — QOL-042 has no code path that writes to `debates` or `arguments`; the `link_columns_immutable` trigger proves the link itself is immutable except for `is_removed`. **Soft-remove only** (no DELETE policy). Plain language — no internal codes; "argument" not "debate", never "game"; "settled" the only end-state word; no "access denied" as an error. The pure models import no React / Supabase / network / AI and read no `Date.now()`.
- **QOL-039 soft dependency — degraded path:** QOL-039 (public/private visibility) is **not built** — `public.debates` has no `visibility` column. Per design §11 the §7 policies and the `link_target_must_be_locked` trigger use `is_debate_open_or_locked` + `is_debate_participant` + `is_moderator_or_admin` alone (today's behaviour — every open/locked room is content-readable, so every link resolves to `authorized`); the `title_only` chip state is dead-but-harmless code, still written and tested. When QOL-039 lands a one-line follow-up migration swaps in the visibility-aware source-readability helper.
- **+137 tests / +7 suites.** Full suite **8521 tests / 303 suites passing** (from the 8384 / 296 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean. New suites: `linkedPriorArgumentModel.test.ts`, `linkedPriorArgumentCopy.test.ts`, `argumentRoomLinksApi.test.ts`, `qol042Migration.test.ts`, `oneBoxRootClaimLink.test.ts`, `inspectPopoutLinkedPrior.test.ts`, `qol042NoForbiddenImports.test.ts`.
- **Operator follow-up (deploy is a separate operator action):** `npx supabase db push --linked` to apply `20260521000010_qol042_argument_room_links.sql`; verify with `npx supabase db lint` + `npx supabase db status`. **No Edge Function deploy** — QOL-042 adds none. No env var, no secret, no `.env` change, no dependency install. If QOL-039 ships *after* QOL-042, the operator also applies the one-line follow-up migration swapping the source-readability helper to the visibility-aware variant.

## QOL-032 — Inspect popout (node & evidence detail) (Epic 8 — Timeline Interaction Mechanics)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review — the **Inspect popout**, the strictly read-only node / evidence / branch detail surface ("understand what is here") rendered through the QOL-030 flash-popout chassis. Inspect is the *understand* surface — it never authors, posts, or edits anything; its single bridge is the §5 "Suggested next move" hand-off, which closes Inspect and opens the **Act popout** (QOL-031). QOL-032 converges SC-002 (timeline node popover) and SC-003 (sidecar) directly into the popout. **No migration, no Edge Function, no `supabase/` change** — QOL-032 is UI-only client composition. No service-role, no direct insert, no new dependency, no Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no `.env` touched. Issue #201.

- **What it ships:** The production code shipped in the branch build commit (`ce802c4`): `src/features/arguments/oneBox/inspectPopoutModel.ts` — the pure-TS content model. `buildInspectPopout(input)` produces the **fixed seven-section set** (design §3.2 — §1 What this move says · §2 Why it matters · §3 What is unresolved · §4 Where it sits · §5 Suggested next move · §6 Semantic flags · §E Evidence detail) with the LIFE-001 **stage-driven emphasis** applied (design §3.3): the stage-emphasised section is pulled to slot 0 and expanded by default — emphasis only **re-orders**, it never removes a section, so `sections.length` is always 7. Each section's body resolves to plain language; an absent input renders an explicit §7 "nothing here" fallback (`No evidence attached.` / `No semantic flags.`), never a blank section. The §5 hand-off carries one `ActEntryId` per stage; in an archived room the hand-off chip is disabled with the reason "This argument is settled." while Inspect itself stays fully functional. `InspectPopout.tsx` — the render component on the shipped `Popout` / `PopoutGroup` / `PopoutEntry` chassis; it consumes `buildInspectPopout` unchanged and renders the collapsible section rows, the §5 hand-off chip, the optional settled banner, and a `‹ prev / next ›` traversal row (wrap disabled at root / latest, consistent with IX-003). The QOL-030 chassis files and the sibling popouts (Act / Go) are untouched.
- **What this card finishes:** the design §8 test suite — the build commit shipped the model + component but no tests. Two new suites cover §8 in full: `inspectPopoutModel.test.ts` (206 — the fixed seven-section set always all-present; the §3.3 stage-emphasis table for every `PointLifecycleState` incl. the doctrine test that emphasis only re-orders and never removes a section; the §5 narrative-frame table S1 F3/F5/F10 + S2 F3/F5/F9; the §5 suggested-move `ActEntryId` per stage; the read-only contract — the model exposes only sections + one hand-off descriptor + a banner flag; the §7 edge cases — node with no evidence, no semantic flags, archived room; no raw `snake_case` / verdict copy in any rendered string; determinism + purity). `inspectPopoutComponent.test.tsx` (62 — chassis use, the fixed section set rendered, the §3.3 emphasised section first + expanded, the read-only contract asserted at the render boundary, the §5 hand-off closes Inspect + opens Act, the §7 edge cases incl. own-node identical role-agnostic render and prev/next wrap-disabled, chassis a11y, the no-write doctrine + ban-list).
- **Doctrine encoded:** Inspect is **strictly read-only** — `InspectPopout.tsx` imports no Supabase / network / AI / router primitive, renders no `<TextInput>` / `onChangeText`, takes no compose / submit / `onDirectAction` / `onRoleChange` prop; its single action is the §5 hand-off, which only **names** an `ActEntryId` for the host and closes Inspect. **Plain language only** — every rendered string is plain English; no internal code / `snake_case` reaches a section title or body (RULE-001). **No verdict / winner / loser / true / false copy** — §3 "What is unresolved" describes the *move*, never the person; the settled banner states the argument is "settled", never declares a result. **Read-only is universal** — there is no own-node special case (unlike Act); the component carries no viewer-role branch. Deterministic pure projection over already-built models (META-001, LIFE-001, RULE-001/003, EV-001) — `inspectPopoutModel.ts` re-derives none of them, holds no React / Supabase / network / AI import, and reads no `Date.now()`.
- **+268 tests / +2 suites.** Full suite **8384 tests / 296 suites passing** (from the 8116 / 294 baseline). Typecheck + lint clean. No production defect was found — the build commit's `inspectPopoutModel.ts` / `InspectPopout.tsx` are unmodified by this card.
- **No operator step** — pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. QOL-032 is the last of the QOL-030 popout-expansion cards (Act / Inspect / Go) — all three now build complete.

## QOL-031 — Act popout (the flash menu) (Epic 8 — Timeline Interaction Mechanics)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review — the **Act popout**, the universal contextual action menu ("what can I do here") rendered through the QOL-030 flash-popout chassis. QOL-031 is the **render layer** for QOL-030's shipped `buildActPopout` 3-gate pure function — it does **not** re-derive the model; it renders the model's output. **No migration, no Edge Function, no `supabase/` change** — QOL-031 is UI-only client composition. No service-role, no direct insert, no new dependency, no Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no `.env` touched. Issue #200.

- **What it ships:** New `src/features/arguments/oneBox/ActPopout.tsx` — the Act popout render component on the shipped `Popout` / `PopoutGroup` / `PopoutEntry` chassis (the sibling of QOL-033's `GoPopout.tsx`). It consumes the 3-gate `buildActPopout` output unchanged and renders it: the group order is fixed (`Respond · Evidence · Resolve · Structure · Direct · Participation`, exactly as the model emits it); the §3.4 stage-promoted entry is visually emphasized via the chassis `isPromoted` styling (raised surface + heavier text + ★ marker); a host-supplied `disabledEntries` map renders a model-surviving but contextually-unavailable entry **disabled with a one-line reason** — never a silent omission (the §7 wireframe's "Flag — disabled: can't flag your own"). Three entry kinds dispatch to host callbacks — `box_opening` re-types the OneBox, `direct` fires an immediate action through existing Edge Functions / RLS, `role_change` changes the seat and re-opens the popout (§3.2). The load-bearing render decision is extracted into the pure `buildActRenderGroups` helper so the repo's `.tsx` UI-test discipline can exercise it without a renderer. `OneBox.tsx` is rewired (minimal registration) to render `<ActPopout>` instead of its prior inline `Popout` + `PopoutGroup` block; the QOL-030 chassis files (`boxModel.ts`, `Popout.tsx`, `PopoutEntry.tsx`, `PopoutGroup.tsx`, `actPopoutModel.ts`) are untouched.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the stage gate **only orders** — it never removes a valid entry; that is the model's job, the render layer renders the result and emphasizes the promoted entry, nothing more (a promoted entry that is also host-disabled drops the promotion — a disabled row cannot be a suggested move). A **disabled entry always shows why** — no silent omission (the engine + role gates inside `buildActPopout` *remove* invalid / forbidden entries; the render layer's `disabledEntries` map handles the narrower role-blocked-with-reason case the design §3.3 / §7 / §8 calls out). The convergence of SC-001 (side action rail) / SC-004 (timeline node dock) / RULE-005 (channel chip row) **reuses the shipped models** — `ActPopout` calls `buildActPopout` and forks no gate (no `applyEngineGate` / `applyRoleGate` / `applyStageGate` re-implementation). Deterministic pure render projection — `ActPopout.tsx` imports no Supabase / network / AI / router primitive, never writes to `public.arguments`, uses no service-role, reads no `Date.now()`; the direct entries that mutate (Flag, Make-private, governance) route through host callbacks to the existing Edge Functions / RLS. No verdict / winner / loser / true / false copy — every entry label comes from `actPopoutModel` (already ban-list scanned); the one literal string `ActPopout` authors (the §8 zero-entry note) joins the shared `oneBoxCopyBanList` doctrine scan.
- **+75 tests / +1 suite.** Full suite **8116 tests / 294 suites passing** (from the 8041 / 293 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean. New suite: `actPopoutComponent.test.tsx` (69 — chassis use, fixed group order, the §3.4 promoted-entry emphasis, disabled-entries-visible-with-a-reason, the entry-kind → chassis-kind mapping, the §6 narrative-frame table reproduced as 8 frames + the §8 edge cases, the §5 convergence, the no-write doctrine, the kind dispatch + OneBox registration, the doctrine ban-list, render-projection faithfulness). `oneBoxCopyBanList.test.ts` extended (+7) to scan the Act render layer's empty-state copy + an `ActPopout.tsx` import-purity scan.
- **No operator step** — pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. QOL-031 is the first of the QOL-030 popout-expansion cards; QOL-033 (Go) already shipped, QOL-032 (Inspect) remains.

## QOL-033 — Go popout (navigate & re-view) (Epic 8 — Timeline Interaction Mechanics)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review — the **Go popout**, the navigate-and-re-view surface that plugs into the QOL-030 flash-popout chassis (the third popout beside Act / Inspect). Go moves the viewport and reconfigures the board's render mode — it performs **no write and no content mutation**. **No migration, no Edge Function, no `supabase/` change** — QOL-033 is UI-only client composition. No service-role, no direct insert, no new dependency, no Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no `.env` touched. Issue #202.

- **What it ships:** New `src/features/arguments/oneBox/goPopoutModel.ts` — the pure-TS Go content model (the navigate-and-re-view twin of `actPopoutModel.ts`). `buildGoPopout(input)` produces the four design §3.2 control groups — **Jump** (Root · Latest · Hot zone · Branch list) · **View** (Timeline ⇄ Cards) · **Density** (Compact · Normal · Expanded) · **Lens** (Active path · Unresolved · Evidence) — with each entry's `isActive` + `isDisabled` + `disabledReason` resolved against the current view / density / lens and the IX-002 `timelineMiniMapModel`. New `src/features/arguments/oneBox/GoPopout.tsx` — the render component on the shipped `Popout` / `PopoutGroup` / `PopoutEntry` chassis; it embeds the IX-002 `TimelineMiniMap` strip **read-only** (passes the already-built model straight through; below IX-002's node threshold the strip is omitted with a one-line note). The QOL-030 chassis files are untouched — QOL-033 only *consumes* the chassis.
- **Doctrine encoded:** Go performs **no write, no content mutation** — every entry only reconfigures the viewport or the render mode (`GoPopout.tsx` imports no Supabase / network / AI / router; a source-scan test proves it). A focus **lens dims, never hides** — the lens entries only select a `GoLens`; the actual dimming is IX-001's `applyTimelineLens`, whose `LensEmphasis` has no `hidden` value, so a lens structurally cannot remove a node (a test verifies the §3.3 stage tables through `applyTimelineLens`: Unresolved → `needs_response`, Evidence → `evidence_requested`, Active path → IX-001's topology `activePathLens` helper; a zero-match lens leaves the board unfiltered). The **hot zone** is the IX-002 `findHotZone` longest warm/hot run — an **activity** signal chosen by run length, never "hottest", never correctness; the Go model never re-derives it. Density / lens are **timeline-only** — in Cards view every density + lens entry is disabled with a visible "Available in Timeline view" reason; the Branch-list entry disables with "No side branches yet" when no side branch exists. Deterministic pure projection — `goPopoutModel.ts` holds no React / Supabase / network / AI import and no `Date.now()`. No verdict / winner / loser copy in any label — the QOL-033 group headings, entry labels, accessibility labels and disabled reasons join the shared `oneBoxCopyBanList` doctrine scan.
- **+100 tests / +2 suites.** Full suite **8041 tests / 293 suites passing** (from the 7941 / 291 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean. New suites: `goPopoutModel.test.ts` (68 — jump-target resolution, hot-zone-by-activity, branch-list disabled-with-reason, density preserves the entry set + timeline-only-in-Cards, lens §3.3 stage membership, lens dims-never-removes, zero-match lens, mini-map threshold, the §6 edge cases, determinism + purity), `goPopoutComponent.test.tsx` (22 — chassis use, the embedded read-only mini-map, the no-write doctrine, reduce-motion threading, lens-dims-never-hides copy). `oneBoxCopyBanList.test.ts` extended (+10) to scan the Go popout strings + a `goPopoutModel` import-purity scan.
- **No operator step** — pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. QOL-033 is the third and last of the QOL-030 popout-expansion cards (Act / Inspect / Go).

## QOL-030 — One-box composer + flash-popout chassis (Epic 8 — Timeline Interaction Mechanics)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review — the **one-box composer foundation** the MVP interaction surface stands on. A single switchable composer "box" identified by `(type, target, view)`: a flash menu switches type, per-type draft buffers make type-switching non-destructive, and the box composes into both Timeline and Cards view rather than being replaced by a bespoke screen. **No migration, no Edge Function, no `supabase/` change** — QOL-030 is client composition over existing data; posting stays on the existing `submit-argument`. No service-role, no direct insert into `public.arguments`, no new dependency, no Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no `.env` touched. Issue #199.

- **What it ships:** New `src/features/arguments/oneBox/` module — `boxModel.ts` (the `BoxType` / `BoxTarget` state machine over `(type, target, view, stageContext, lifecycle, draftBuffers)` plus `renderSchema`; per-type draft buffers so switching type never destroys a draft), `actPopoutModel.ts` (`buildActPopout` — the 3-gate pure function: engine hard-filter ∩ role hard-filter ∩ stage soft-promotion), the reusable popout chassis `Popout.tsx` / `PopoutEntry.tsx` / `PopoutGroup.tsx` (the RN primitives QOL-031/032/033 will later consume), and `OneBox.tsx` — the box component that re-types itself. `ArgumentComposerDock.tsx` refactored to host the OneBox; posting stays on `submit-argument`. QOL-031/032/033 popout *contents* remain placeholders pending their own cards.
- **Doctrine:** the box is one mounted component that re-types itself — never swapped for a bespoke input screen. The flash menu offers only engine-valid (Constitution transition table) and role-allowed box types. Pure-TS models (`boxModel.ts`, `actPopoutModel.ts`) hold no React / Supabase / network import; the constitution engine is untouched. No `game` / `Debates` / `Tap to join` vocabulary in any touched normal-user copy. No bespoke surface is retired in this card (CreateDebateForm / JoinDebatePanel re-housing is a named later follow-up).
- **+171 tests / +3 suites.** Full suite **7861 tests / 289 suites passing** (from the 7690 / 286 baseline). Typecheck + lint clean.
- **No operator step** — pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. **Unblocks QOL-031 / QOL-032 / QOL-033** (the Act / Inspect / Go popouts that consume this chassis).

## IX-001 — Timeline density + focus lenses (Epic 8 — Timeline Interaction Mechanics)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review — the pure **density + lens core** consumed by the already-shipped Conversation Gallery (Epic 11) and the future QOL-033 in-room Go popout. **IX-001 ships NO screen** — per design §0/§1 it is the pure model plus a tiny session-state hook; the gallery screen and QOL-033 *render* it. No standalone IX-001 React shell was built (deliberate — the design explicitly honours "build the pure model, not a standalone IX-001 shell"). **No migration, no `supabase/` change, no Edge Function, no new dependency.** No Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no service-role, no `.env` touched. Issue #20.

- **What it ships:** New pure-TS model `src/features/arguments/timelineDensityLensModel.ts` (no React, no Supabase, no network, no AI, no `Date.now()` — recency uses an injected `ctx.nowMs`). Density: `GalleryDensityMode` is a **strict superset** of VG-004's shipped 3-mode `TimelineDensityMode` — `expanded` / `normal` / `compact` map 1:1 by the same name, plus a 4th *gallery-only* `scan` tier; `TimelineDensityMode` is **not forked** and gains no 4th value. `toTimelineDensityMode` clamps `scan → compact` so an in-room node never renders tighter than 28px (hit targets stay ≥44px). `GALLERY_DENSITY_SPECS` is a descriptive per-mode card spec (excerpt line clamps, which optional regions render); `scan` hides only *optional* regions (mini-timeline, stats row), never data. Lenses: 11 named `FocusLensId` values plus the `none` baseline; `GALLERY_LENS_PREDICATES` (each a deterministic boolean over a built `ConversationGalleryCard`, every lifecycle-driven predicate carrying a pre-LIFE-001 fallback to always-present fields) and `TIMELINE_LENS_PREDICATES` (the 7-lens node subset over `ArgumentTimelineMapNode`, with the gallery-only room-level lenses absent from `TIMELINE_LENS_IDS`); `activePathLens` is the separate topology helper. `applyGalleryLens` / `applyTimelineLens` tag every item `bright | dimmed` and never change list length; a zero-match lens forces every item back to `bright` with `isEmpty: true`. `GallerySortAxis` (the 3 coarse axes) maps to the shipped `ConversationSortMode` via `toConversationSortMode`. `DensityLensViewConfig` + `applyViewConfigChange` encode the page-reset rules (search/sort reset the page; density/lens do not). New `src/features/arguments/useDensityLens.ts` — a thin session-state hook holding one `DensityLensViewConfig`; the **only** IX-001 file importing React. Both re-exported additively from `src/features/arguments/index.ts`.
- **Doctrine encoded:** a density mode and a focus lens are **view state only** — neither is ever an input to the Constitution engine, `argumentScoreModel`, `antiAmplification`, or any validation gate. A focus lens **dims, never deletes** — `LensEmphasis` has no `hidden` value, so a lens structurally cannot remove an item from the data set; a dimmed item stays a full, navigable control. Heat/density are **activity** signals, never verdicts — `heating_up` / `hot` read `ConversationGalleryCard.heatLevel` (whose source is already "active friction, not popular") and the lens copy says so out loud ("activity, not a result" / "momentum, not a result"). No authored string contains a verdict or popularity token — a ban-list test scans every `FOCUS_LENS_COPY` string against the repo's canonical `_forbiddenLifecycleTokens`; no internal snake_case code reaches user-facing copy. The model file holds no popularity-shaped identifier and the constitution engine is untouched.
- **+129 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite **7690 tests / 286 suites passing** (from the 7561 / 282 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate + terminology-audit clean. New suites: `timelineDensityLensModel.test.ts` (the 4 density modes + spec object, all 11 gallery lens predicates incl. the lifecycle-loaded and lifecycle-absent fallback branch of every lifecycle-driven predicate, the 7 timeline lens predicates, `applyGalleryLens`/`applyTimelineLens` invariants, the sort + density converters, `applyViewConfigChange` reset rules, determinism, the documented one-card-per-conversation dedupe rule), `timelineDensityLensNoVerdict.test.ts` (the doctrine ban-list + heat-is-activity disclaimers + no popularity identifier), `timelineDensityLensForbiddenImports.test.ts` (source scan: model is pure, imports type-only, `TimelineDensityMode` still has exactly 3 members), `useDensityLens.test.ts` (hook contract via its pure delegate logic + a structural source scan).
- **No operator step** — pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. **Blocks QOL-033** (the Go popout renders this model's density modes + `TIMELINE_LENS_IDS`). The Conversation Gallery screen does not yet *consume* the model — wiring the Density + Lens controls into `ConversationGalleryScreen` is a follow-up surface task (design §9.2); IX-001's deliverable is the pure core, which is consumable today.

## QOL-037 — Evidence applicability dispute flow (Epic 6 — Evidence)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review — adds the **evidence applicability axis**: a structured way to dispute *what* a piece of evidence applies to (which month a payment covers, which obligation a receipt settles), separate from disputing that the evidence exists (EV-001 `SourceChainStatus`) or that a source/quote was *asked for* (EV-003 evidence debt). QOL-037 ships the behaviour spec for the QOL-030 `respond_to_evidence` box type — it produces **no standalone surface**; it is content plugged into QOL-030's `renderSchema` and read by the QOL-032 Inspect popout. Render-time-derived: **no migration, no `evidence_applicability` table, no new RLS policy**. The one Edge Function touch is a **minimal advisory pass-through** in `submit-argument` (§7.4 of the design). No Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no service-role, no direct `public.arguments` insert, no `.env` touched, no dependency install. Issue #206.

- **What it ships:** New pure-TS model `src/features/evidence/evidenceApplicabilityModel.ts` — `EvidenceResponseChoice` (the closed seven-choice set: `accept` / `accept_with_caveat` / `dispute_date` / `dispute_amount` / `dispute_applicability` / `request_source` / `request_clarification`), `ApplicabilityStatus` (the three-rung axis: `applicability_undisputed` / `applicability_disputed` / `applicability_supported`), the `EvidenceResponseRecord` advisory block, the frozen `EVIDENCE_RESPONSE_CHOICES` descriptor table + `ALL_EVIDENCE_RESPONSE_CHOICES` / `ALL_APPLICABILITY_STATUSES`, `MIN_CLARIFICATION_CHARS = 12`. Five public functions: `validateEvidenceResponseDraft` (the non-`accept` → clarification-required validation rule), `deriveApplicabilityStatus` (the render-time status derivation from the chronological response history), `previewApplicabilityTransition` (the box preview line), `summarizeApplicabilityChip` (the plain-language chip contract), `buildRespondToEvidenceViewModel` (the full box view-model incl. the QOL-032 §E claimed-vs-disputed read fields). New `evidenceApplicabilityCopy.ts` — every choice label/helper, both applicability chip labels/helpers, both disabled-Post reasons, the preview-line and read-view strings, all frozen, with `ALL_EVIDENCE_APPLICABILITY_STRINGS` so the ban-list test scans the whole surface. New RN components `RespondToEvidenceForm.tsx` (the seven-choice radio set + conditional required-clarification field + status-preview line + own-evidence / observer role gates; plugs into QOL-030's `renderSchema('respond_to_evidence', …)`) and `ApplicabilityChip.tsx` (the applicability-axis status chip — text label + tone token, self-hides when `applicability_undisputed`; renders alongside the EV-002 receipt chip so both axes show at once). Barrel `src/features/evidence/index.ts` additively re-exports the model + copy + components. `MoveDraftPatch` (`src/features/arguments/conversationMoves.ts`) gains an optional `evidenceResponse?: MoveEvidenceResponse` field — optional, so all existing callers are unaffected.
- **Doctrine encoded:** an applicability dispute changes a **status, never a verdict** — `dispute_applicability` flips `applicability_undisputed → applicability_disputed`; the model has deliberately **no** "applicability proven / disproven / true / false" value (no truth-negative state by design). Copy is "Applicability disputed" / "Applicability supported", never "proof" / "true" / "false" / "winner" / "loser" / "verdict" / "case closed" — a ban-list test scans every QOL-037 system-generated string for the verdict + amplification + person-attribution token lists and the `looksLikeInternalCode` snake_case predicate. The three axes never collapse: existence/source-chain (EV-001), obligation/debt (EV-003), and applicability (QOL-037) are computed independently and never read each other — a test asserts `dispute_date` / `dispute_amount` / `accept_with_caveat` / `request_source` / `request_clarification` never touch `ApplicabilityStatus`. `applicability_supported` is reachable **only** via corroborating *moves* (an `accept` of the contested point by the disputing party, or an explicit `corroboratedByArgumentIds` move id) — never via heat, replies, views, or popularity (anti-amplification). The clarification-required rule is a **validation** gate (it may disable Post, always with a visible plain-language reason — no silent no-op); it is not a score gate, and score never blocks. The model is pure TS — no React, no Supabase, no network, no AI, no `Date.now()`. The constitution engine is untouched; the seven choices route to existing argument types and QOL-037 adds **no new Constitution transition**.
- **The one Edge Function change — minimal and advisory:** `supabase/functions/submit-argument/index.ts` accepts an optional `evidence_response` block on the request body and copies it **verbatim** into the `server_validation` JSONB snapshot it already writes (`supabase/functions/_shared/validationSchemas.ts` gains a permissive optional `EvidenceResponseSchema`). The function does **not** validate it, does **not** hard-block on it, does **not** branch the insert path on it — a malformed block can never block a post; the existing body validation is the only gate, unchanged. This keeps the applicability axis render-time-derivable: the client reads `evidenceResponse` blocks off the argument rows it already fetches and runs `deriveApplicabilityStatus`. No new RLS, no migration, no service-role, no new insert path.
- **+174 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite **7561 tests / 282 suites passing** (from the 7387 / 278 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate + terminology-audit clean (audit: 0 live prohibited). New suites: `evidenceApplicabilityModel.test.ts` (full line + branch coverage — choice-set shape, the validation rule, the derivation table incl. order-independence and the unknown-choice degradation, the transition preview, the chip contract, the view-model, the verdict / amplification / snake_case ban-lists), `RespondToEvidenceForm.test.tsx` (radio selection, clarification show/hide, Post disabled-with-reason, draft-buffer preservation, own-evidence + observer gates, accessibility, rendered-text ban-list), `ApplicabilityChip.test.tsx` (per-status render, hidden-when-undisputed, color-independence, ban-list), `submitArgumentEvidenceResponse.test.ts` (the advisory pass-through contract — block copied verbatim, never a hard block). Integration touch in `conversationMoves.test.ts` (the new optional `evidenceResponse` field leaves existing patch behaviour unchanged).
- **Operator follow-up (out of scope for this card — deploy is a separate operator action):** `npx supabase functions deploy submit-argument --linked` so the function knows to pass the new optional `evidence_response` field through into the validation snapshot. The deploy is **backward-compatible** — the field is optional, so an older client that omits it is unaffected. Until the deploy lands, the box still works (the move body posts) but the applicability status would not persist for other viewers. **No migration**, no new RLS policy, no new Edge Function directory, no env var, no `.env` change, no dependency install. QOL-030 (`respond_to_evidence` box chassis) and QOL-036 (`claimedApplicability` metadata) are upstream cards: per design §11 the form degrades gracefully where they are not yet built — `claimedApplicability` renders "Not specified" and `request_source` still posts as an ordinary clarification when EV-003 debt tracking is absent.

## QOL-036 — Payment / screenshot evidence metadata object (Epic 6 — Evidence)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review — an **additive extension** of the EV-001 `EvidenceArtifact` so a payment / transfer screenshot can be attached as a *structured* object (amount, date, redacted payer/payee, note, claimed applicability, a `confidence` pinned to `user_asserted`) instead of being pasted as un-disputable free text into the argument body. **Adapter-only**, per EV-001's path (b): **no migration, no `argument_evidence_artifacts` table, no Edge Function, no `submit-argument` change, no RLS change**. No Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no Supabase write, no service-role, no `.env` touched, no dependency install. Issue #205.

- **What it ships:** Extends the pure-TS model `src/features/evidence/evidenceModel.ts` — appends `payment_screenshot` (the seventh `EvidenceArtifactKind`), the `EvidenceConfidence` type (one value, `user_asserted`) + `ALL_EVIDENCE_CONFIDENCES` + `PINNED_PAYMENT_CONFIDENCE`, the sub-shapes `EvidenceAmount` / `PaymentParty` / `ClaimedApplicability`, the optional `PaymentEvidenceMetadata` sub-object on `EvidenceArtifact` (every field optional except the pinned `confidence`), and the optional `payment` field on `EvidenceAttachmentInput`. New helpers: `detectRawAccountData` (conservative 12–19 digit-run / IBAN-shape / routing-shape heuristic), `findRawAccountDataFields` (throw-free guard returning offending dotted field paths), `redactPaymentParty` (masks account-data runs to `•••• ` + last 4; role-only inputs pass through), `getPaymentEvidenceLabel` ("Payment record"), `summarizePaymentEvidence` (one-line redaction-safe summary). `classifyEvidenceKind` gains the payment branch (an explicit `kind` still wins); `isAttachmentEmpty` now counts `payment` as a fourth non-empty field; `buildEvidenceArtifacts` runs the redaction guard (raw account data → strip the `payment` sub-object + downgrade kind to `screenshot_redacted`), pins `confidence` to `user_asserted`, normalises the amount (negative → 0, NaN → absent), and clamps every text field. Barrel `src/features/evidence/index.ts` additively re-exports the new types + helpers.
- **Doctrine encoded:** a payment object is **inert** — it carries no truth value and emits **no** `PointStandingDelta` (`evidenceModel.ts` imports nothing from `src/features/pointStanding/` — a forbidden-imports test proves it). Existence ≠ applicability: `amount` / `paidAt` / `noteText` / `claimedApplicability` are separate axes so a QOL-037 dispute can target one precisely; QOL-036 stores only the *claimed* side. `confidence` is pinned to `user_asserted` and the interface carries no `verified` / `confirmed` / `proven` / `valid` / `isTrue` / `truthValue` field (structural test). **No raw financial account data — ever:** the adapter rejects (strips, never masks-and-stores) a `payment` object whose fields carry a card / account / routing / IBAN digit shape; a `JSON.stringify` digit-run scan proves no 12+ digit run survives a degraded artifact. A payment artifact runs the existing EV-001 source-chain table over `(url, sourceText, quote)` only — alone it yields `unverified`, never auto-promoting to `source_and_quote` / `primary_present`. The change is strictly additive — every existing `EvidenceArtifact` field keeps its name/type, and EV-002 / EV-003 / EV-005 / `ReceiptChip` / the timeline contract compile and behave identically (the one existing test that asserted "exactly six kinds" is updated to "exactly seven" — the unavoidable enum-extension test-update the design's §11 calls for). All QOL-036 system-generated strings are plain English, ban-list-asserted (no `proof` / `true` / `winner` / `case closed`, no amplification or person-attribution token). Pure TS — no React, no Supabase, no network, no `Date.now()` / `new Date()`.
- **+98 tests / +1 suite.** Full suite **7387 tests / 278 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate + terminology-audit clean (audit: 0 live prohibited). New suite `paymentEvidenceMetadata.test.ts` (full line + branch coverage — type/enum coverage, `classifyEvidenceKind` payment branch, the adapter payment path, the redaction guard, redaction degradation, `redactPaymentParty`, amount normalisation, field clamping, `summarizePaymentEvidence` / `getPaymentEvidenceLabel`, receipt-chip + timeline integration, the no-truth / no-standing doctrine anchors, the ban-list, source purity). One existing test updated in `evidenceModel.test.ts` (six → seven kinds).
- **No operator step** — pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. Downstream wiring (threading the `payment` object into the `submit-argument` request) is owned by the QOL-030 `add_evidence` box submit path or the EV-001 path-(c) persistence card — QOL-036 is consumable as a pure model today.

## EV-003 — Evidence debt tracker (Epic 6 — Evidence)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review — adds the **obligation axis** of the evidence model. EV-001 modelled the evidence *artifact* (existence / source-chain) and EV-002 gave it an inspection surface + a way to *ask*; EV-003 closes the ask loop by tracking whether a source / quote / receipt / context request was ever answered. Render-time-derived: **no migration, no `evidence_debt` table, no Edge Function, no `submit-argument` change**. No Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no Supabase write, no service-role. Issue #16.

- **What it ships:** New pure-TS model `src/features/evidence/evidenceDebtModel.ts` — `EvidenceDebt` (a structural obligation record), `EvidenceDebtKind` (5: `source` / `quote` / `receipt` / `context` / `primary_record`), `EvidenceDebtStatus` (8: `requested` / `supplied` / `challenged` / `accepted_by_participant` / `accepted_by_both` / `unresolved` / `stale` / `branched`), the per-node + per-room roll-up types, the `EvidenceDebtChipContract`. `deriveEvidenceDebts` derives every debt in a room from its argument rows (recognised request tag → opens a debt; later moves in the requested subtree resolve / challenge / branch / decline it; the close-condition table reads EV-001's `sourceChainStatus` only as a kind-named threshold; a still-`requested` debt past `STALE_DEBT_THRESHOLD_DAYS`=7 goes `stale`). `getNodeEvidenceDebtSummary` / `getRoomEvidenceDebtSummary` / `summarizeEvidenceDebtChip` / `getNodeEvidenceDebtChip` are pure roll-ups. New RN component `src/features/evidence/EvidenceDebtChip.tsx` — the obligation-axis status chip, rendered on the timeline node beside the EV-002 receipt chip (a node can show both axes at once); non-pressable, self-hides on a node with no debt. Wiring: `timelineNodePopoverModel` + `TimelineNodePopover` render the chip; `ArgumentGameSurface` derives the room debts once per render (reusing the EV-002 artifact map + tag map — no new fetch) and threads a per-node summary into the popover via a new `evidenceDebtSummaryFor` prop on `ArgumentTimelineMap`; the conversation gallery card gains an `evidenceDebtSummary`, an open debt is the authoritative `source_chain_fight` signal, and "Evidence requested" / "Source still owed" card signals appear.
- **Doctrine encoded:** an evidence debt is a **structural obligation marker**, never a verdict — an open debt means "this point lacks X", never "this point is wrong"; a resolved debt is "settled", never "proven" / "case closed". The model is **advisory**: it imports nothing from `src/features/pointStanding/` (emits no `PointStandingDelta`) and nothing from the constitution validator (never enters `evaluateArgumentDraft`, never a flag, never disables Post — a node with five open debts is just as postable-onto as one with none). It reads no heat / engagement / view / follower field — a debt's status is a pure function of *moves*. Pure TS — no React, no Supabase, no network, no `Date.now()` (the staleness clock is injected). The gallery precision fix: a room whose `source_request` debts all resolved is kept *out* of the source-trail lane (a tag count alone could not tell open from resolved). All chip / status-line copy is plain English, ban-list-asserted (no `proof` / `true` / `winner` / `case closed` / amplification / person-attribution tokens; `settled` is used at discharge).
- **+142 tests / +2 suites.** Full suite **7289 tests / 277 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + terminology-audit clean (audit: 0 live prohibited). New suites: `evidenceDebtModel.test.ts` (full line + branch coverage — derivation, resolution scan per kind, staleness, roll-ups, chip copy, worst-status ordering, graceful degradation, doctrine anchors, ban-list), `EvidenceDebtChip.test.tsx` (pure-helper + source-scan). Integration touches in `timelineNodePopoverModel.test.ts`, `argumentGameSurface.test.ts`, `conversationGalleryModel.test.ts`.
- **No operator step** — pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install.
