## QOL-026 — Fix Admin All Arguments loader (Behavior Repair Wave / QOL — admin data layer)

**Status:** Complete — the Admin → All Arguments loader no longer requests columns that do not exist on `public.arguments`. Issue #137.

- **Why this card exists:** the Admin → All Arguments tab was fully broken — it showed "Could not load argument activity" with detail `column arguments.selected_tag_codes does not exist`. The loader at `src/features/admin/adminArgumentsApi.ts` requested **two columns that have never existed** on `public.arguments` in the same `.select()` call: `selected_tag_codes` and `attached_evidence`. PostgREST reports unknown columns one at a time, so fixing only the first would leave the page broken on the second.
- **Fix — two columns, two treatments:**
  - `selected_tag_codes` → replaced with a correct PostgREST nested embed `argument_tags(tag_code)`. Tags live in the existing `public.argument_tags` join table (admins already have RLS SELECT). A new exported pure helper `asTagCodes` flattens the embed into `AdminArgumentRow.selectedTagCodes` (`string[] | null`), so the category/qualifier badge derivers now receive real tag data instead of the broken `null`.
  - `attached_evidence` → dropped entirely. There is no evidence table or column to join to. `hasEvidence` and the evidence badge (which had never shown real data) were removed cleanly rather than hardcoded to `false`; a future `EV-*` Evidence card reintroduces an evidence indicator deliberately against a real table.
- **Modified files (3 production + 2 test):** `src/features/admin/adminArgumentsApi.ts` (`.select()` list, `RawArgumentRow`, new `asTagCodes` helper, `.map` result), `src/features/admin/types.ts` (`hasEvidence` removed from `AdminArgumentRow`), `src/features/admin/AdminArgumentsTab.tsx` (evidence badge + unused `evidence` palette entry removed); `__tests__/adminArguments.test.ts` (query-shape contract assertions for both removed columns + the new embed) and new `__tests__/adminArgumentsTagJoin.test.ts` (`asTagCodes` unit tests + type contract).
- **Doctrine:** tags are advisory category/qualifier signals, never truth verdicts; removing the evidence badge removes a signal, adds no verdict. SELECT-only loader on the shared anon RLS-scoped `supabase` client — no migration, no Edge Function, no service-role, no AI path. Non-admin access stays blocked by the existing RLS on `arguments` + `argument_tags` and the `AdminScreen` tab gating.
- **+15 tests / +1 suite.** Full suite **4623 tests / 160 suites** (4604 passing). Typecheck + lint clean. The 19 failing tests across 5 xAI/bot-fixture suites (`xaiSeededStancesLive`, `xaiAdversarialProvider`, `xaiAdversarialSourceHarvest`, `xaiAdversarialPipeline`, `aiDrivenBotCorpus`) are pre-existing and environmental (missing `.env.engagement-intelligence` in this environment) — unrelated to this card and outside its scope.
- **No operator step** — pure client-code change, no `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration. After merge, the operator should verify in the running app that Admin → All Arguments loads without the `selected_tag_codes` / `attached_evidence` errors and that rows + category/qualifier badges render.

## META-1A — Persisted manual-tag ledger (Release 6.8 / Epic Rules UX / Metadata)

**Status:** Complete — `point_tags` table migration, `apply-manual-tag` Edge Function, Deno eligibility mirror, client wrapper, and room-shell loader extension all delivered and green. Migration written-not-applied; Edge Function written-not-deployed (operator runs both post-merge). Issue #76.

- **Why this card exists:** META-001 shipped the manual-tag vocabulary + eligibility matrix but only as an *in-memory* ledger — a tag a participant applied lived in React state, vanished on reload, and was invisible to everyone else. META-1A elevates the manual-tag ledger to a persisted, shared gameplay artifact.
- **Deliverables (8 new files):**
  - `supabase/migrations/20260517000009_meta_1a_point_tags.sql` — the `point_tags` table (9 columns incl. `removed_at` soft-delete + `removed_by`; `tag_code` `CHECK IN` listing the 10 META-001 `ManualTagCode` values verbatim; FKs to `debates` / `arguments` / `public.profiles`), two partial indexes on active rows, a partial unique index `point_tags_one_active_per_tagger`, RLS enabled, and exactly 3 named policies (`pt_insert_eligible`, `pt_select_read_access`, `pt_update_soft_delete`) — **no `for delete` policy** (soft-delete only).
  - `supabase/functions/apply-manual-tag/index.ts` — the single write path. Two actions (`apply` / `remove`), CORS / JWT verify, caller-scoped client for the argument lookup + insert/update, server-side eligibility enforcement, service-role client used **only** for a best-effort `admin_audit_events` row. A duplicate apply (`23505`) is idempotent; `remove` soft-deletes via `removed_at` (admins may remove others' tags).
  - `supabase/functions/_shared/pointTagEligibility.ts` — the Deno-side mirror of META-001's `MANUAL_TAG_ELIGIBILITY_TABLE` + `isApplyAllowed` (Edge Functions cannot import from `src/`); guarded against drift by `pointTagsEligibilityMirror.test.ts`.
  - `src/features/metadata/pointTagsApi.ts` — client wrappers `applyManualTag` / `removeManualTag` (route through `supabase.functions.invoke`), the `PersistedPointTag` interface, and the pure `persistedTagsToManualTagEntries` adapter.
  - 4 new test suites (`pointTagsMigration`, `applyManualTagEdgeFunction`, `pointTagsApi`, `pointTagsEligibilityMirror`) — 64 tests, including the 80-case eligibility matrix executed directly against the mirror's `isApplyAllowed`.
- **Modified files (6):** `argumentsApi.ts` (`fetchArgumentRelations` now reads active `point_tags`), `arguments/types.ts` (`pointTags` on `ArgumentRelations`), `useArgumentRoomMessages.ts` (`pointTagsByArgumentId` map), `ArgumentGameSurface.tsx` (replaced the empty `manualTagsByMessageId` placeholder with the hydrated map; exposes the write-path wrappers), `ArgumentTreeScreen.tsx` (threads the prop), plus `composerHandoff.ts` / `useArgumentViewport.ts` / `argumentCache.test.ts` updated for the additive `pointTags` field on `ArgumentRelations`.
- **Read path is live; write-trigger UI is a noted follow-up.** No tag-apply UI control exists yet (the SC-004 / TimelineNodeActionDock `mark_moved_on` affordance is v1-disabled). META-1A wires the persisted-tag **read path** (the room shell hydrates persisted tags) and exposes `applyManualTag` / `removeManualTag` so a thin follow-up card can wire the apply trigger. The card's "UI reflects persisted state" criterion is met by the read path.
- **Doctrine encoded:** a manual tag is a participant gameplay annotation, never a verdict — the `point_tags` table has no count / score / engagement column; the doctrine ban-list test scans the migration, the function, and the mirror. The Edge Function is the only write path (the room-shell `select` is the documented read exception); soft-delete only — no `.delete()` on `point_tags` anywhere, no `for delete` RLS policy. No AI call, no service-role in client code, no new dependency.
- **+64 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite passes **4608 tests / 159 suites** (4544 / 155 pre-card baseline + this card). Typecheck + lint clean. No existing test broke; `argumentCache.test.ts` literals were extended with `pointTags: []` because `ArgumentRelations` gained the additive field.
- **Operator step (post-merge, in this exact order):** (1) `npx supabase db push --linked` to apply the migration, then (2) `npx supabase functions deploy apply-manual-tag --linked`. Order matters — the function writes to `point_tags`. No env var / secret is introduced.

## IX-003 — Keyboard and accessibility navigation (Release 6.7 / Epic 8 Interaction)

**Status:** Complete — pure-TS keyboard-traversal model, web `onKeyDown` wiring on the argument timeline, screen-reader label upgrade, and tests all delivered and green. Issue #22.

- **Why this card exists:** the horizontal argument timeline (`ArgumentTimelineMap.tsx`) was operable only by touch, and its node screen-reader label was missing two of the four signals the card requires — strength and branch. IX-003 makes the timeline fully keyboard-operable on web and completes the per-node accessibility contract, with no change to the native touch path.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/arguments/keyboardNavigationModel.ts` — new pure-TS model (no React / Supabase / network / AI). `resolveTimelineNavEffect` is the traversal resolver: Arrow L/R walk the chronological prev/next node (no wrap at the ends), Home/End jump to root/latest, Enter/Space resolve to `open_detail` for the active node, Escape resolves to `close_overlay` only when an overlay is open; with no active node Left/Home go to root and Right/End go to latest. `buildNodeAccessibilityLabel` is the single source of truth for the plain-language node label — it now exposes type, side, ordinal, **strength** (`STANDING_BAND_SOFT_LABEL`, plain-language gameplay standing — never a verdict) and **branch** (`deriveBranchLabel`: mainline / side branch / detached). The model inlines the chronological prev/next index logic so its dependency on `argumentGameSurfaceModel` stays type-only — no runtime import cycle.
  - `__tests__/keyboardNavigationModel.test.ts` (60 tests) — pure-model coverage: arrow traversal, Home/End, cold-start (null active), Enter/Space, Escape, unhandled keys, empty/single-node/detached edge cases, no-mutation guard, `isTimelineNavKey`, `deriveBranchLabel`, and `buildNodeAccessibilityLabel` including a per-band strength assertion (all 9 bands) and a verdict-token ban-list test.
  - `__tests__/ix003KeyboardA11yWiring.test.ts` (13 tests) — source scan: `ArgumentTimelineMap` wires the model in (`onKeyDown`, `Platform.OS === 'web'` guard, `preventDefault`, Prev/Next `accessibilityState` disabled, `tabIndex`), keeps the node `accessibilityRole="button"` + `selected` contract, adds no new dependency, and `keyboardNavigationModel` stays React-free with a type-only dependency on `argumentGameSurfaceModel`.
- **Modified files (2):** `src/features/arguments/ArgumentTimelineMap.tsx` (web-only `onKeyDown` + `tabIndex=0` on the timeline group `<View>`; `tabIndex=-1` on node Pressables so the Tab sequence is one stop; Prev/Next gain a disabled `accessibilityState` + dimmed style at the ends; `NodeDot` builds its label via the shared helper); `src/features/arguments/argumentGameSurfaceModel.ts` (Pass 4 now calls the same `buildNodeAccessibilityLabel` helper so the model's stored label and the rendered label never drift).
- **Scope:** keyboard nav drives the SAME `onActivate` / `handleInfoTap` callbacks tap already uses — no parallel selection path. All key handling is `Platform.OS === 'web'`-guarded; native is untouched (tap + VoiceOver/TalkBack rotor). Up/Down arrow keys are explicitly out of scope (deferred — risks colliding with page scroll). No new npm dependency — web key capture uses RN-web's existing `onKeyDown` / `tabIndex` props, spread via a `Platform.OS === 'web' ? {...} : {}` object (no `as` cast).
- **Doctrine encoded:** the screen-reader "strength" exposure is plain-language gameplay standing (`STANDING_BAND_SOFT_LABEL`), never a verdict — a ban-list test locks it. Keyboard nav only changes *selection*; it cannot post, score, flag, or block. No Supabase, no migration, no Edge Function, no AI path, no service-role.
- **One existing test updated:** `__tests__/argumentTimelineMapRootOnboarding.test.ts` — the node label format changed (`position N of M` replaces `Message N of M`, plus strength / branch / "opening claim"), so the one assertion against the old string was updated to the new format. This is a design-anticipated label change, not a regression. No other existing test changed.
- **+73 tests / +2 suites.** Full suite passes **4544 tests / 155 suites** (4471 / 153 pre-card baseline + this card). Typecheck + lint clean.
- **No operator step** — pure code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no dependency.
- **Browser verification:** IX-003 is a visible-UI card; the design's §"Browser verification checklist" (14 items — Expo web + keyboard + screen reader) is a human pass to walk before merge.

## PR-002 — Profile tag popout (Release 6.7 / Epic 9 Profile)

**Status:** Complete — closed-vocabulary profile-tag feature, ProfileTagPopout Modal, preferences-popout entry row, App wiring, and tests all delivered and green. Issue #24.

- **Why this card exists:** a signed-in user had no way to add lightweight identity-light profile tags (interests, debate style, availability, accessibility self-description). PR-002 ships an optional, doctrine-safe tag picker reached from a new row inside PR-001's "My preferences" popout.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/profileTags/` — new feature module, 8 files: `profileTagModel.ts` (pure TS — the versioned `ProfileTagSelection` blob, `schemaVersion: 1`, `MAX_PROFILE_TAGS = 5`, defensive `mergeTagSelectionWithDefaults`, immutable `toggleTag` / `canAddTag` / `isTagSelected` / `getTagsByCategory` / `resolveTagLabel` / `selectedTagDefinitions`); `profileTagVocabulary.ts` (the frozen, closed, curated 28-tag vocabulary across 4 categories — 10 topic interests, 8 debate styles, 5 availability, 5 accessibility self-description); `profileTagsStorage.ts` (AsyncStorage glue — best-effort load/save, never throws, runs every load through `mergeTagSelectionWithDefaults`); `useProfileTags.ts` (hook — loads the blob, optimistic `toggleTag` / `clearTags`); `profileTagCopy.ts` (all user-facing strings); `ProfileTagChip.tsx` (multi-select chip — `accessibilityRole="checkbox"`, check glyph + filled style, ≥44 hit target); `ProfileTagPopout.tsx` (core `Modal` bottom-sheet reusing the `PreferencesPopout` / `DeletionRequestSheet` pattern); `index.ts` barrel.
  - The vocabulary is **closed by doctrine design** — there is no free-text tag entry and no "custom / other" escape hatch anywhere; users select only from the fixed 28-tag set. This is the mechanism that makes the card's DISALLOWED list (protected-class / party-affiliation / unverified-"expert" / hostile-label / ideology-personality-scoring tokens) exhaustively test-enforceable.
- **Persistence:** device-local AsyncStorage, one versioned JSON blob keyed `cdiscourse:profile-tags:<userId>` — a SEPARATE blob from PR-001's preferences blob (different shape, different defensive-parse need). No migration, no Supabase column, no Edge Function, no service-role, no AI path.
- **`MAX_PROFILE_TAGS = 5` enforced in three places:** on read (`mergeTagSelectionWithDefaults` truncates an over-cap stored blob), in the model (`toggleTag` is a no-op when adding past the cap), and in the UI (unselected chips disable at the cap). Tags are optional — 0 is valid, there is no floor.
- **v1 visibility:** tags are device-local and **self-visible only** — they appear in the user's own popout. There is no other-user profile surface in the app; shared/other-user visibility is an explicit v2 follow-up (a Supabase column + RLS + an other-user profile screen). The `schemaVersion` field keeps that migration path open.
- **Doctrine encoded — proven by tests:** profile tags never affect truth / score / heat / point standing and never change validation gates. `profileTagValidationImmutability.test.ts` runs the real Constitution engine (`validateTransition` / `validateDepth` / `validateBodyLength` / `runDeterministicChecks`), `argumentScoreModel.computeStatementStanding`, and `antiAmplification.applyAntiAmplification` twice — once with no tag state and once after a full 5-tag selection is persisted to AsyncStorage — and asserts byte-identical (`JSON.stringify`) output; it also source-scans both directions of import isolation (no gate module imports `profileTags`; no `profileTags` file imports a gate/score/validation module). `profileTagVocabularySafety.test.ts` exhaustively scans every id and label in the 28-tag vocabulary for protected-class / party / "expert" / hostile-label / verdict tokens and confirms no `TextInput` exists in the popout or chip. `profileTagDoctrine.test.ts` covers the copy verdict ban-list, internal-code leak, role-escalation surface, secrets, and accessibility scans.
- **Modified files (3):** `src/features/session/sessionKeys.ts` (new `profileTagsKey` builder, mirrors `userPreferencesKey`); `src/features/preferences/PreferencesPopout.tsx` (one new "Profile tags" `Pressable` row — `pref-field-profile-tags` / `pref-profile-tags-open` — plus `onOpenProfileTags` + `profileTagCount` props; still exactly one `TextInput`, so PR-001's `preferencesDoctrine.test.ts` stays green); `App.tsx` (mounts `useProfileTags` + `<ProfileTagPopout>` as a second core `Modal` in the signed-in shell).
- **+87 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite passes **4471 tests / 153 suites** (4384 / 149 pre-card baseline + this card). Typecheck + lint clean. No existing test required a change — PR-002 is purely additive plus two back-compatible props on `PreferencesPopout`.
- **No operator step** — pure code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no new dependency (the React Native AsyncStorage package was already in `package.json` via PR-001).
- **Browser verification:** PR-002 is a visible-UI card; the design's §"Browser verification checklist" (15 items) is a human Expo-web pass to walk before merge.

## PR-001 — "My preferences" popout (Release 6.7 / Epic 9 Profile)

**Status:** Complete — device-local preferences feature, Modal bottom-sheet, app wiring, and tests all delivered and green. Issue #23.

- **Why this card exists:** a signed-in user had no lightweight way to inspect or adjust their own profile/UI preferences without leaving the game. PR-001 ships a header-gear-opened bottom-sheet of nine fields.

  - `src/features/preferences/` — new feature module: `userPreferencesModel.ts` (pure TS — the versioned `UserPreferences` blob, `schemaVersion: 1`, defensive `mergeWithDefaults`, immutable `applyPreferencePatch`, the `resolveEffectiveReduceMotion` compose helper, `densityToTimelineMode`, `isHighContrast`); `preferencesStorage.ts` (AsyncStorage glue — best-effort load/save, never throws); `useUserPreferences.ts` (hook — loads the blob, reads OS reduce-motion, optimistic `updatePreference`); `preferencesCopy.ts` (all user-facing strings, centralised for the ban-list scan); `PreferencesPopout.tsx` (the core `Modal` bottom-sheet, reusing the `DeletionRequestSheet` pattern — no new dependency, no router drawer); `PreferenceRow.tsx` (reusable segmented-control + toggle primitives); `GeneratedAvatar.tsx` (deterministic initials-on-hashed-colour placeholder); `index.ts` barrel.
  - The nine fields: display name (account write via existing `updateOwnDisplayName`), avatar preview (generated placeholder — PR-003 owns real upload), contact email (read-only display + honest "can't change here yet" note — the email-change flow is PR-004), notification preference (honest non-functional stub — v1 has no push), default room entry, visual density, colour accessibility mode (`default`/`high_contrast` have real effect; the 3 colour-blind sim modes persist-but-inert with honest "coming" copy), reduce motion, default side label (persist-only with honest copy — no central side-label resolver exists to wire into yet).

- **VG-004 density wire:** VG-004 had already soldered `resolveNodeGapPx(input.density)` into `buildArgumentTimelineMap` and `ArgumentGameSurface` already passed `density: 'normal'` literally. PR-001 replaces that literal with the user's preference, threaded `App.tsx → ArgumentTreeScreen → ArgumentGameSurface`. The reduce-motion preference (OS value composed with the user's `system`/`on`/`off` override) is threaded the same path into `ArgumentTimelineMap`, replacing its independent OS read when supplied.
- **Doctrine encoded:** exposes no role / admin / moderation control; captures no secret, token, or auth field; the preferences module imports no score / engine / validation module — a preference is cosmetic and never reaches a gate. All copy passes the verdict ban-list; option labels are human prose (no internal-code leak).
- **+63 tests / +2 suites.** Full suite passes **4384 tests / 149 suites** (4321 / 147 pre-card baseline + this card). Typecheck + lint clean. No existing test required a change — PR-001 is purely additive plus optional back-compatible props on three argument-room components.
- **No operator step** — pure code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no new dependency (AsyncStorage `2.2.0` was already in `package.json`).

Each fixture is run through `buildArgumentTimelineMap` and asserted against the design's invariant table.

It is — `buildPointLifecycleMap` takes `{ timelineMap, artifactsByMessageId }`, and AN-002 fixtures satisfy both (`artifactsByMessageId` is an empty `Map`). All 3 were kept.
- **Doctrine encoded:** no verdict / truth tokens (winner / loser / correct / true / false / liar / etc.) in any fixture body, label, or descriptor — fixtures use neutral low-stakes topics (bike lanes, remote work, street trees); no popularity / engagement signal; dev/QA-only — a structural test asserts no `app/` file imports `visualQaFixtures`. Pure model, no Supabase / migration / Edge Function / service-role / AI path. AN-001 / AN-003 untouched and not imported.

## AN-003 — Tree playability diagnostics (Release 6.7 / Epic 13 Analytics)

**Status:** Complete — pure model, test suite, and the §5 dev-script snapshot generator all delivered and green. Issue #66.

- **Why this card exists:** GAME-001 shipped exhaustion / moved-on advisories with v1 threshold constants. AN-003 produces a deterministic, verdict-free `TreePlayabilityDiagnostics` record so an operator can look at real rooms and see whether those thresholds are firing sensibly — is the lifecycle-mapped tree playable, where is it stuck, and what advisory state dominates.
- **Deliverables (this card):**
  - `src/features/analytics/treePlayabilityDiagnostics.ts` — new pure-TS deriver (no React / Supabase / network / AI / clock). `computeTreePlayabilityDiagnostics`, `TreePlayabilityClass` (`empty` / `healthy` / `unresolved_dominant` / `stalled` / `mixed`), `TreePlayabilityDiagnostics` + input/config types, `DEFAULT_TREE_PLAYABILITY_CONFIG`, `renderTreePlayabilityMarkdown` (pure string builder, no file I/O), `_forbiddenTreePlayabilityTokens`, and an `_internal` namespace for test access. Consumes the already-built `PointLifecycleMap`, `ArgumentTimelineMapModel`, GAME-001 advisories, EV-001 contracts, and SC-004 dock models — never re-derives any of them. Does NOT import AN-001's `boardDiagnostics.ts` (non-duplication is a card acceptance criterion).
  - `__tests__/treePlayabilityDiagnostics.test.ts` — new pure-model suite, 29 tests: empty/deterministic/total counts, unresolved + exhausted/stale derivation, `branch_recommended` excluded from both sets, branch overload + max/median depth, active-unresolved-point reachability, evidence-debt concentration (with and without an EV-001 contract), the no-actionable-suggestion dock scan + detached-node exclusion, dominant-advisory GAME-001 + lifecycle-fallback paths, playability classification, fraction guards, the verdict-token ban list, the no-duplication structural assertion against AN-001, and purity. Fixtures are inline consts including a 55-node / 36-cluster deep tree.
- **R1 (`node.depth` semantics) resolved:** `buildArgumentTimelineMap` sets `depth = 0` for roots and `parent.depth + 1` for replies — depth is ABSOLUTE from the timeline root, so cluster-relative depth = `node.depth - clusterRoot.depth` (the design's assumption). Pinned by test #8.
- **D7 adapted metric implemented:** SC-004's dock always keeps `open_cards_detail` enabled so a literally-empty dock is unreachable; AN-003 counts non-root, non-detached nodes whose dock has no enabled POST-producing action instead. D5 honored — the breakdown iterates the exported `ALL_POINT_LIFECYCLE_STATES` (19 entries).
- **Doctrine encoded:** no verdict tokens in any produced string; no popularity / engagement / heat / standing input anywhere; pure model, no Supabase / migration / Edge Function / service-role / AI path; AN-001's `boardDiagnostics.ts` untouched and never imported.
- **§5 dev-script delivered (mechanism: `tsc` precompile, no new dependency):** the revised §5 of `docs/designs/AN-003.md` is now implemented. `scripts/diagnostics/buildTreePlayabilitySnapshot.ts` (authored in TypeScript) builds the four consumed models from a room fixture via the shipped builders (`buildArgumentTimelineMap`, `buildPointLifecycleMap`, `buildExhaustionTimeoutInputFromLifecycle` + `deriveExhaustionTimeoutAdvisory`, `getTimelineEvidenceContract`, `buildMoveMetadataLedger`, `buildTimelineNodeActionDockModel`), then calls AN-003's `computeTreePlayabilityDiagnostics` + `renderTreePlayabilityMarkdown` — it re-derives nothing. A standalone `tsconfig.diagnostics.json` (CommonJS-targeted; does NOT extend the Expo-based root tsconfig, which carries an incompatible `customConditions`) compiles the script + its verified React-Native-free closure to the gitignored `artifacts/diagnostics/tree-playability-build/` dir; a bare `node` run then emits the snapshot to the gitignored `artifacts/diagnostics/tree-playability/` tree. Four npm scripts added (`diagnostics:tree-playability:build` / `:dry` / `:fixture` / base). `eslint.config.js` `ignores` gained `artifacts/**` so the generated emit dir is never linted. No new dependency — `typescript` was already a devDependency. `npm run typecheck` (root tsconfig), `npm run lint`, and `npm run test` are untouched by the diagnostics tsconfig.
- **+29 tests / +1 suite** (delivered earlier; §5 is non-test, purely additive). Full suite passes **4287 tests / 146 suites**. Typecheck + lint clean. No existing test required a change — AN-003 is purely additive.
- **No operator step** for the merged code. Optional QA convenience: `npm run diagnostics:tree-playability:dry` prints a snapshot to stdout; `npm run diagnostics:tree-playability -- --fixture <room.json>` writes one to the gitignored `artifacts/` tree.

## VG-004 — High-tech board visual polish without new dependencies (Release 6.6 / Epic 2 Visual Grammar)

**Status:** Complete (pure client UI — no operator step). Issue #113.

- **Why this card exists:** the horizontal argument board (`ArgumentTimelineMap`) read as a flat form. VG-004 adds six render-only refinements so it reads as a playable map: a node-level active-path glow, a selected-node halo, an evidence "receipt" inner mark, a branch-stub glyph refinement, a tone tint on active-path nodes, and density-aware inter-node spacing.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/arguments/timelineNodeVisualModel.ts` — new pure-TS model (no React / Supabase / network). `TimelineDensityMode`, `TIMELINE_NODE_GAP_BY_DENSITY`, `resolveNodeGapPx`, `deriveTimelineNodeVisualStyle`, `NodeGlowTier`, `TimelineNodeVisualStyle`.
  - `src/features/arguments/ArgumentTimelineMap.tsx` — `NodeDot` gains the active-path glow, selected-node halo, evidence receipt mark, and tone-tint `<View>` layers, all derived via the pure helper. New reduce-motion state reads `AccessibilityInfo.isReduceMotionEnabled()` with a `reduceMotionChanged` subscription and the existing try/catch discipline. New `StyleSheet` entries `nodeGlow` / `nodeHalo` / `nodeToneTint` / `receiptMark` / `receiptMarkInner`.
  - `src/features/arguments/BranchCollapseStub.tsx` — new pure helper `buildBranchCollapseStubLabelParts`; the stub now renders a decorative branch-kind glyph + the count as two `<Text>` spans (glyph hidden from screen readers).
  - `src/lib/designTokens.ts` — extended (not replaced) with `GLOW` (active-path indigo + selected cream halo) and `RECEIPT_MARK` (reuses the `ARGUMENT.evidence` family). `TOKENS` aggregate gains `glow` + `receiptMark`.
  - `src/features/arguments/argumentGameSurfaceModel.ts` — `BuildTimelineMapInput` gains optional `density?: TimelineDensityMode`; `xStep` now calls `resolveNodeGapPx(input.density)`.
  - `src/features/arguments/ArgumentGameSurface.tsx` — passes `density: 'normal'` explicitly.
  - `__tests__/argumentNodeVisualVG004.test.ts` — new pure / style-rule suite (47 tests) covering `resolveNodeGapPx`, glow / halo / receipt / tone-tint derivation, doctrine strength-independence, the `accessibilityFragment` ban-list, `buildBranchCollapseStubLabelParts`, token assertions, source-scan invariants, the VG-001 contract, and density-preserves-active-node.
- **Operator Q1 — answered (option b):** the default board density was deliberately loosened. `TIMELINE_NODE_GAP_BY_DENSITY = { compact: 28, normal: 44, expanded: 64 }`; `resolveNodeGapPx(undefined) === 44`. The exported `TIMELINE_NODE_GAP` constant was changed `28 → 44` to stay consistent with the new `'normal'` default (it had exactly one consumer — line 1206 of the same file — which now calls `resolveNodeGapPx`).
- **Doctrine encoded:** the glow + halo are strength-independent — they read only navigation / selection state, never `standingBand` / `heat` / any score. The tone tint is the only field reading `toneBand` / `temperatureBand`; it is applied to active-path nodes only and capped at alpha ≤ 0.18. Every new state has a non-color signal (geometry / stroke / text) and a plain-English `accessibilityFragment` with zero verdict / amplification / snake_case tokens. No new color token (reuses existing hex). No `react-native-svg`, no new npm dependency. No Supabase / migration / Edge Function / AI path. VoiceOver / TalkBack verification of the new announcements is a deferred follow-up per `accessibility-targets`.
- **+47 tests / +1 suite.** Full suite passes **4258 tests / 145 suites** (4211 / 144 pre-card baseline + this card). Typecheck + lint clean. One existing test updated: `__tests__/designTokens.test.ts` — the `TOKENS` aggregate key-set assertion now expects the two new VG-004 categories (`glow`, `receiptMark`). No timeline x-coordinate test required a change: `argumentTimelineMap.test.ts` asserts node `x` only with relative comparisons (`toBeLessThan` / `toBeGreaterThan` / two-map equality), never hardcoded literals, so the 28→44 default gap change did not break any assertion.
- **No operator step:** pure client UI. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration.

## QOL-024 — Admin user invite/create workflow (Release 6.5 / admin tooling)

**Status:** Complete (code-only — Edge Function deploy is an operator step). Issue #110.

- **Why this card exists:** the admin Create-user form could only mint an already-confirmed user with a password — there was no path that emails a new human tester a self-serve first-sign-in link, forcing the operator to hand-issue credentials out-of-band.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `supabase/functions/admin-users/index.ts` — new `handleInviteUser` handler + `case 'invite_user'` in the switch. Uses `inviteUserByEmail` (not generate-link) so the invite link/token never enters function memory or the response; the response is `{ ok, invited, notification }` only — no link, token, email, or userId.
  - `supabase/functions/_shared/adminSchemas.ts` — new `InviteUser` zod object in the `AdminUsersRequestSchema` discriminated union. `role` is `z.enum(['user','moderator'])` — `'admin'` is rejected (an invite can never mint an admin).
  - `supabase/functions/_shared/adminAudit.ts` — `'invite_user'` appended to `WHITELISTED_ACTIONS`.
  - `supabase/functions/_shared/adminInvitePayload.ts` — new pure, Deno-import-free builders `buildInviteAuditPayload` / `buildInviteResponse`. The audit payload stores `emailDomain` (domain only, never the raw email) and `redirectToProvided` (boolean, never the URL).
  - `src/lib/edgeFunctions.ts` — `'invite_user'` added to the client `AdminUsersAction` union.
  - `src/features/admin/adminApi.ts` — new `adminInviteUser` wrapper. Derives the invite callback URL via `buildAuthRedirectUrl({ kind: 'invite' })` with the same fail-soft try/catch as `adminSendPasswordReset`; passes an explicit field list (no `...input` spread).
  - `src/features/admin/adminHelpers.ts` — `adminErrorMessage` maps the `invite_email_not_configured` code to plain operator-directed copy; new pure UI helpers `isInvitingHuman` / `isModeToggleVisible` / `isPasswordFieldVisible` / `resolveCreateUserDispatch`.
  - `src/features/admin/AdminCreateUserForm.tsx` — new Invite/Password mode toggle for the human branch (invite is the default); invite mode hides the password field and shows an "Invite sent." status line. The Human/Bot toggle and the entire Bot branch are untouched.
  - 3 new test suites: `adminInviteUserClient.test.ts` (12), `adminInviteUserAuditShape.test.ts` (14), `AdminCreateUserForm.test.tsx` (22); `adminSchemas.test.ts` extended with the `InviteUser` mirror (+4).
- **Doctrine encoded:** an invite can only create `user` / `moderator` — `admin` is a 422 at schema validation. No service-role in client code (the invite call runs on the service client built inside the Edge Function, after the admin check). No invite link / token / raw email / userId in the response or any log. Audit row stores `emailDomain` + `redirectToProvided` only. Plain-language copy — the user never sees `invite_user` / `invite_email_not_configured`. Fail-soft — a bad redirect origin degrades to no `redirectTo`, never blocks the invite.
- **No migration:** verified `admin_audit_events.action` is a `text` column (not a Postgres enum), so the new audit action needed only a JS-array edit. No xAI / Anthropic / X API calls; no Supabase write by Claude; no real email sent; no new dependency.
- **+52 tests / +3 suites.** Full suite passes **4211 tests / 144 suites** (4159 / 141 pre-card baseline + this card). Typecheck + lint clean. No existing tests required changes.
- **Operator follow-up (post-merge):** the feature is effective only after the operator runs `npx supabase functions deploy admin-users --linked` and enables the Supabase "Invite user" email template + the `/auth/callback` redirect allow-list entry. See `docs/admin-email-validation-plan.md` § "QOL-024 — admin user invite-by-email runbook". No `db push`.

## QOL-023 — Supabase auth redirect helper (Release 6.5 / deployment hardening)

**Status:** Complete. Auth emails sent by Supabase (signup confirmation, magic link, password reset, admin-triggered reset) now carry an `emailRedirectTo` / `redirectTo` pointing at the deployed origin instead of the dashboard `localhost` Site URL. Issue #109.

- **Why this card exists:** `signUpWithEmailPassword` never passed `emailRedirectTo`, so a user invited to the deployed dev app received a link pointing at `http://localhost:8081` and bounced — onboarding was broken in the deployed environment.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/lib/auth/buildAuthRedirectUrl.ts` — new pure-TS helper (no React / Supabase / network imports). `buildAuthRedirectUrl(input)` deterministically computes the redirect URL from a runtime origin + `isDev` flag. Origin-resolution fallback (runtime origin → hosted fallback `https://dev.cdiscourse.com` in non-dev → `http://localhost:8081` only in a true dev build). Scheme/host validation (rejects `file:`/`javascript:`/`data:`/`vbscript:`/`blob:` in every build; rejects `http://` in non-dev; rejects hostless origins). Normalization (trim, strip trailing slashes, lowercase scheme + host, preserve port, discard path). Exports `AuthRedirectKind`, `DEFAULT_AUTH_ROUTES`, `DEV_FALLBACK_ORIGIN`, `HOSTED_FALLBACK_ORIGIN`, `InvalidAuthRedirectOrigin` (error carries only a `reason` enum, never the offending origin string).
  - `src/lib/auth/resolveRuntimeOrigin.ts` — new impure boundary. `resolveRuntimeOrigin()` reads `window.location.origin` → `__CDISCOURSE_RUNTIME_ENV__.EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN` → `process.env.EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN`. `getIsDev()` fail-closes to `false` when `__DEV__` is undefined.
  - `src/features/auth/authApi.ts` — `signUpWithEmailPassword` passes `options.emailRedirectTo`; new exported `sendPasswordResetEmail(email)` wrapper; `mapAuthError` gains a `redirect_invalid` branch; private `safeBuildRedirect` catches `InvalidAuthRedirectOrigin` and degrades to `null` (Supabase falls back to the dashboard Site URL — a bad origin never blocks signup). Exports `REDIRECT_INVALID_MESSAGE` plain-language copy.
  - `src/features/auth/types.ts` — `'redirect_invalid'` added to the `AuthError` union.
  - `src/features/admin/adminApi.ts` — `adminSendPasswordReset` derives a default `redirectTo` from `buildAuthRedirectUrl` when the caller omits it (signature unchanged; the `admin-users` Edge Function already forwards `redirectTo` — no Edge Function change).
  - `src/lib/supabase.ts` — `CDiscourseRuntimeEnv` + `readRuntimeEnv()` gain the optional `EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN` field.
  - `scripts/build/inject-runtime-env.{mjs,ps1,sh}` + `scripts/runtime/server.mjs` — extend the HOST-001b runtime-env injector with an optional `--app-origin` / `-AppOrigin` flag + `EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN` env read; new `looksLikeHttpOrigin` validator (exit 10 on garbage); the `looksForbidden` secret-shape check covers the new value; absence is NOT a build failure (the helper fallback covers it).
  - `.env.example` — adds the `EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN=` key name (empty placeholder; a public URL, not a secret).
  - `docs/admin-email-validation-plan.md` — appends the QOL-023 redirect-URL operator runbook to the Supabase / Auth settings checklist.
  - 4 new test suites: `__tests__/buildAuthRedirectUrl.test.ts`, `__tests__/authApiRedirect.test.ts`, `__tests__/noLocalhostInProdAuthPaths.test.ts` (static scan with a vacuous-pass guard), `__tests__/buildAuthRedirectUrl.doctrine.test.ts`.
- **Doctrine encoded:** Fail-soft — a bad runtime origin degrades (`emailRedirectTo` omitted), never blocks signup. The redirect origin is a PUBLIC URL, never read from `.env*` at runtime. `InvalidAuthRedirectOrigin` carries only the reason enum (no origin leak into logs). Plain-language copy (`redirect_invalid` → "We couldn't open that link…") with no internal code. No service-role anywhere in client code. `buildAuthRedirectUrl.ts` imports nothing.
- **No xAI, Anthropic, or X API calls; no Supabase writes; no service-role; no migration; no Edge Function change; no new dependency. The `admin-users` Edge Function was read-only confirmed (it already forwards `redirectTo`).**
- **+54 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite passes 4159 tests / 141 suites with zero failures (4105 / 137 main baseline + this card). Typecheck + lint clean. (The xAI / engagement-intelligence suites are gated on the gitignored operator file `.env.engagement-intelligence`; they pass in a working tree that has it and fail only in a fresh worktree that does not — this card does not touch those scripts.) One existing test updated: `__tests__/hostOneBuildScripts.test.ts` — the runtime-env shim source-scan assertion was updated to match the refactored `buildRuntimeEnvFileContents` (now assembles an `env` object then `JSON.stringify(env)` so the optional `EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN` key is included only when present). The JSON-encode safety property still holds.
- **Operator follow-up (post-merge):** the feature is end-to-end effective only after the operator (1) sets Supabase Dashboard Auth → URL Configuration Site URL = `https://dev.cdiscourse.com` and adds `…/auth/callback` + `…/auth/reset` to Additional Redirect URLs, and (2) sets the Cloud Run `EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN` secret. See `docs/admin-email-validation-plan.md` § "QOL-023 — auth redirect URL configuration". No `db push`, no `functions deploy`.

## LIFE-1B — Retire `moveAddsAxisInformation` deprecated alias (Release 6.6 / Wave 3 cleanup)

**Status:** Trivial cleanup that retires the JSDoc-deprecated runtime alias `moveAddsAxisInformation` introduced alongside LIFE-001's canonical `hasAdditiveAxisInformation`. Issue #73.

- **Why this card exists:** LIFE-001 shipped both `hasAdditiveAxisInformation` (canonical, clearer name) and a JSDoc-deprecated `moveAddsAxisInformation` alias that simply forwards to the canonical helper. The LIFE-001 review flagged the alias as removable "right after GAME-001" to avoid two-name confusion in downstream consumers (SC-004 / ST-002 / GAME-001). GAME-001 has landed using only the canonical name, so the alias has zero callers in `src/` or `__tests__/` and can be removed safely.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/lifecycle/pointLifecycleAdvisoryInputs.ts` — removed the deprecated alias `export function moveAddsAxisInformation(...)` definition. `hasAdditiveAxisInformation` is now the only additive-axis helper.
  - `src/features/lifecycle/index.ts` — removed `moveAddsAxisInformation` from the barrel re-export list.
- **Doctrine encoded:** None — pure naming hygiene. The canonical `hasAdditiveAxisInformation` semantics are untouched. GAME-001's `exhaustionTimeoutModel.ts` was already using `hasAdditiveAxisInformation`, not the alias, so it is unaffected.
- **Boundary enforcement:** No semantic change. No new helper, no helper signature change, no doctrine surface change. `grep -r moveAddsAxisInformation src/ __tests__/` returns zero matches after the edit.
- **No xAI, Anthropic, or X API calls; no Supabase writes; no service-role; no migration; no Edge Function change; no new dependency; no `.env*` touched; no hosting file touched; no test file modified (no alias-equivalence test existed); the constitution engine remains sacred.**
- **Test count unchanged at 4083 passing.** The 19 pre-existing xAI / Anthropic / engagement-intel suite failures remain unrelated to this card and operator-gated by missing `.env.engagement-intelligence` in this worktree. Typecheck + lint clean. `skills:validate` clean.
- **No operator follow-up** — pure local change. No deploy step.

## GAME-001 — Point exhaustion + timeout rules (Release 6.6 / Wave 3)

**Status:** Pure-TS sibling deriver landed alongside LIFE-001. New module `src/features/lifecycle/exhaustionTimeoutModel.ts` exports `deriveExhaustionTimeoutAdvisory(input): ExhaustionTimeoutAdvisory` — a fixture-friendly single-purpose advisory deriver for the seven exhaustion / timeout / synthesis advisory states. Issue #64.

- **Why this card exists:** LIFE-001's `composeClusterState` already fires the exhaustion / moved-on / ignored / synthesis-ready states inside its 1.2 KLOC cascade, but it does not accept a flat cluster-level input object, does not accept override thresholds, and pins `synthesis_ready` to the stricter "explicit synthesis-shape move" semantics. AN-003's "sweep thresholds at low cost" diagnostic mode, and SC-003 / ST-002 follow-ups that want the broader "concession + no debt → synthesis_ready" reading, need a standalone deriver — building this on top of LIFE-001 would bloat a file that is already past 1.2 KLOC and blur the canonical-state vs advisory-deriver contracts.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/lifecycle/exhaustionTimeoutModel.ts` — new pure-TS module. `ExhaustionTimeoutAdvisoryState` 7-value union (`synthesis_ready` / `exhausted` / `ignored_by_both` / `ignored_by_affirmative` / `ignored_by_negative` / `moved_on_by_affirmative` / `moved_on_by_negative`). `ExhaustionTimeoutInput` flat 14-field input shape (cluster-level signals + override config + optional upstream state). `ExhaustionTimeoutConfig` with `minClusterAgeForTimeoutAdvisory` floor (default 2) ON TOP OF the four LIFE-001-shared thresholds. `ExhaustionTimeoutAdvisory` output with compile-time-pinned `blocksSubmit: false` + `appliesPointStandingPenalty: false` literal-type fields. `DEFAULT_EXHAUSTION_TIMEOUT_CONFIG` frozen defaults (mirror LIFE-001 for the four shared values). `ALL_EXHAUSTION_TIMEOUT_ADVISORY_STATES` frozen array (iteration order = priority cascade). `deriveExhaustionTimeoutAdvisory` pure / total / deterministic function. `buildExhaustionTimeoutInputFromLifecycle` convenience adapter that pulls the six cluster-level signals from a `PointLifecycleClusterSummary` + members + side-turn sequence + artifact-status map. `_forbiddenExhaustionTimeoutTokens` test-only export (LIFE-001 ban list + GAME-001 amplification / penalty / person-attribution extras).
  - `src/features/lifecycle/index.ts` — barrel re-exports for every GAME-001 public surface.
  - `__tests__/exhaustionTimeoutModel.test.ts` — 103 new tests. 5 fixture suites (exhaustion / one-party ignored / two-party ignored / synthesis-ready / moved-on) with threshold-boundary coverage. No-blocking + no-penalty doctrine pin across every state. Copy ban-list scan (verdict / popularity / amplification / person-attribution tokens forbidden). Person-attribution scan ("the user" / "they ignored" / "Affirmative ignored" forbidden in helper lines). Priority cascade verified by stripping prereqs. N / M / K / J threshold boundaries (N-1 / N / N+1 for each). `minClusterAgeForTimeoutAdvisory` floor pin (defeats the "cluster posted turn 4, by turn 5 no reply → moved_on_by_negative" false-positive). Override-threshold coverage + defaults-parity with LIFE-001. Adapter field-by-field coverage, idempotency, no-mutation, round-trip with the deriver. Purity / determinism / source-scan (no React / Supabase / Anthropic / xAI / fetch / Date / Math.random / process.env / console / engine import).
- **Resolved design questions (designer-confirmed):**
  1. Sibling deriver in a NEW module — LIFE-001's `composeClusterState` is NOT modified.
  2. Input shape is flat: 14 cluster-level fields, no DAG / no member walk. AN-003's threshold sweep runs at constant cost.
  3. `synthesis_ready` broadened to "concession-or-narrowing + no unresolved evidence debt". Coexists with LIFE-001's stricter semantics; consumers choose which one to display.
  4. Reads RULE-003's `LIFECYCLE_UX_MAP` for label + helperLine — never authors copy.
  5. Adapter `buildExhaustionTimeoutInputFromLifecycle` ships in the same module so it shares thresholds.
  6. Priority order: `synthesis_ready > exhausted > ignored_by_both > ignored_by_<side> > moved_on_by_<side> > null`.
- **Doctrine encoded:** `blocksSubmit: false` and `appliesPointStandingPenalty: false` are compile-time-pinned literal-type fields. The deriver returns `null` (no advisory) when upstream state is `archived_or_resolved` / `conceded` / `narrowed` / `confirmed` / `rebutted` / `synthesis_ready` / `sourced` — those upstream states already classify the cluster better than any advisory could. The deriver never authors a plain-language string — every label + helperLine comes from RULE-003. The input shape contains no heat / popularity / engagement / amplification fields. Every produced helper line is scanned for "the user" / "the author" / "the poster" / "your opponent" / verb-form "Affirmative ignored" / "they ignored" patterns. The four shared thresholds inherit from `DEFAULT_LIFECYCLE_ADVISORY_CONFIG` so the two derivers agree out of the box.
- **Boundary enforcement:** Pure / total / deterministic — no `Date.now()`, no `Math.random()`, no module-level mutable state. No import from `src/lib/constitution/engine` (sacred — doctrine §5). No import from React / React Native / Expo / Supabase / Anthropic / xAI / fetch / XMLHttpRequest. No `process.env` read. No `console.*` call. No `submit-argument` / `validation/` import.
- **No xAI, Anthropic, or X API calls; no Supabase writes; no service-role; no migration; no Edge Function change; no new dependency; no `.env*` touched; no hosting file touched; no `pointLifecycleModel.ts` / `pointLifecycleAdvisoryInputs.ts` / `pointLifecycleClusters.ts` / `lifecycleUxMap.ts` / `moveMetadataLedger.ts` / `point-standing/*` source touched. The constitution engine remains sacred.**
- **+103 tests / +1 suite** (3980 → 4083 passing baseline). The 19 pre-existing xAI / Anthropic / engagement-intel suite failures remain unrelated to this card and operator-gated by missing `.env.engagement-intelligence` in this worktree. Typecheck + lint clean. `skills:validate` clean.
- **No operator follow-up** — pure local change. No deploy step. The deriver is NOT auto-wired into any rendered surface; SC-003 / ST-002 / AN-003 follow-up cards plumb it where they want it.

## RULE-002 — Evidence symmetry between validation and visuals (Release 6.6 / Wave 3)

**Status:** Pure-TS UX adapter + ComposerValidationPanel chip render + ArgumentComposer wiring + 67 new doctrine-anchored tests landed. The constitution engine's `FlagCode` vocabulary (16 codes) and the Stage 6.2 / 6.4 advisory codes (7 codes) now map through a single source of truth into render-ready `ValidationActionUx` tuples — `{ code, chipLabel, helperLine, suggestedMove, dockAction, presetKey }` — that surface a one-click chip in the composer validation surface. Issue #33.

- **Why this card exists:** Stage 6.2 made the validation rails advisory (no more hard `OFF_TOPIC` / `PARENT_NONRESPONSIVE` blocks) but the warning rows in `ComposerValidationPanel` stayed plain text. A player who saw "Topic coverage is light." had no one-click way to fix it. RULE-002 routes every engine flag + Stage 6.2/6.4 advisory code into the existing ST-002 / SC-004 / COMPOSER-001 plumbing so the chip pre-seeds the composer with the right move shape.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/rulesUx/validationActionMap.ts` — new pure-TS module. `ValidationActionCode` union (23 entries — every `FLAG_CODES` value + the 7 Stage 6.2/6.4 advisory codes). `ValidationActionUx` interface. `VALIDATION_ACTION_MAP` frozen catalog. `ALL_VALIDATION_ACTION_CODES` frozen array. `getValidationAction(code)` (compile-time exhaustive reader). `mapValidationActionOrSuppress(code)` (defensive normalising reader — returns `null` for unknown / `null` / `undefined` / `''`). `shouldRenderValidationActionChip(action)` (true iff at least one routing field is non-null — codes with no clean repair return false here, suppressing the chip). `_forbiddenValidationActionTokens()` test-only export. NEVER value-imports `constitution/engine` (sacred — doctrine §5); the cross-walk between `FLAG_CODES` and the union is enforced by a runtime test that iterates the engine's enum.
  - `src/features/arguments/ComposerValidationPanel.tsx` — adds optional `onSuggestedMove?: (action: ValidationActionUx) => void` prop, co-located `ValidationActionChip` subcomponent, `chipFor(detail)` derivation. The chip renders **next to** (not in place of) every warning + blocking-error row when the engine flagCode resolves to a chip-emitting `ValidationActionUx`. Codes that suppress (e.g. `invalid_transition`, `civility_risk`, `missing_parent`) keep their engine warning text but render no chip. New `actionChip` / `actionChipText` styles; neutral surface (color is not the only signal — accessibility-targets).
  - `src/features/arguments/ArgumentComposer.tsx` — new `handleValidationAction` callback routes the chip press through the existing `quickActionToPreset(action.presetKey, parentType)` + `handleMovePatch(patch)` pipeline (COMPOSER-001 + EV-002). Adds NO new execution paths. The submit-button gate `canSubmit` is **unchanged** — `evaluationResult?.allowPost ?? false` continues to drive it (doctrine §1).
  - `__tests__/validationActionMap.test.ts` — 67 new tests covering catalog completeness (16 engine + 7 advisory = 23), field-shape & length caps (`chipLabel` ≤ 32, `helperLine` ≤ 80, `looksLikeInternalCode === false`), ban-list (verdict / amplification / person-attribution tokens), issue acceptance criteria (weak_topic → "Sharpen the topic link"; parent_nonresponsive → "Reconnect to parent"; evidence_required → "Attach a source"; source_chain → "Ask for the source"), submit-gate additivity, normalisation parity (uppercase / hyphen / whitespace / `null` / `undefined`), RULE-001 coordination (shared labels match verbatim across the two maps), render contract (chip-emitting vs suppressed codes), code-shape hygiene, doctrine self-check (engine module never value-imported; no `fetch` / Supabase / Anthropic / xAI literal in source).
- **Resolved design questions (designer-confirmed):**
  1. Chip renders in `ComposerValidationPanel`, NOT the SC-004 timeline dock.
  2. No new engine flag codes — the adapter reads existing engine output only. Engine stays sacred.
  3. `parent_nonresponsive` routes to `branch_tangent` `suggestedMove` + `clarify` `dockAction` + `clarify` `presetKey` (ST-002 `preset_gap` pattern; ST-002 has no clarify-shaped `SuggestedMoveCode` in v1).
  4. Codes with no clean repair (`invalid_transition`, `civility_risk`, `missing_parent`, `ad_hominem_possible`, `duplicate_argument_possible`, `excessive_length`, `unclear_claim`, `needs_moderator_review`, `validation_failed_after_retries`) → all-null UX. Chip suppressed; engine warning still renders.
  5. The doctrine-canonical phrase "Popularity is not proof" survives — the `_forbiddenValidationActionTokens()` ban-list scans `\\bpopular\\b` (standalone token), not the noun `popularity`. The `anti_amplification` helper line avoids the standalone `engagement` token by using "Reach does not equal support" instead.
- **Doctrine encoded:** Every produced string passes verdict / amplification / person-attribution ban-list scans (test §3). `looksLikeInternalCode` returns `false` for every chipLabel + helperLine (no `off_topic`-shape internal code leaks). The doctrine-self-check test reads the validationActionMap source file and asserts: no `fetch(`, no Supabase / Anthropic / xAI import, no `process.env.*API_KEY` literal, no React / `useState` / `async` / `await`, no value-import of `constitution/engine`. Score never gates posting (§1) — pinned by a "Ordinary replies remain postable" acceptance test that mounts a synthetic `EvaluationResult { allowPost: true, warnings: [weak_topic_satisfaction] }` and verifies `allowPost` stays `true` after the chip lookup. Popularity is not evidence (§3) — `anti_amplification` and `platform_support_warning` chips route to `ask_source` / "Hold off on scoring", never to "accept because popular".
- **Boundary enforcement:** `validationActionMap.ts` is pure constants + two readers + one boolean helper. No mutable state. No `Date.now()` / `Math.random()` / `fetch` / `anthropic` / `xai`. `ComposerValidationPanel.tsx` source-scan is clean. `ArgumentComposer.tsx` adds one new `useCallback` that delegates entirely to existing functions; no new state, no new effect, no Supabase / fetch.
- **No xAI, Anthropic, or X API calls; no Supabase writes; no service-role; no migration; no Edge Function change; no new dependency; no `.env*` touched; no hosting file touched; no `src/domain/constitution/*` file touched (engine sacred — doctrine §5); no `pointLifecycleModel.ts` / `moveMetadataLedger.ts` / `lifecycleUxMap.ts` / `ruleToUiMap.ts` / `timelineNodeActionDockModel.ts` / `suggestedMovesModel.ts` / `quickActionPresets.ts` source touched (RULE-002 reads their types and frozen exports only).**
- **+67 tests / +1 suite** (3913 → 3980 passing baseline). The 19 pre-existing xAI / Anthropic / engagement-intel suite failures remain unrelated to this card and operator-gated by missing `.env.engagement-intelligence`. Typecheck + lint clean.
- **No operator follow-up** — pure local change. No deploy step.

## GAL-001 — Upgrade gallery sections into scrum-like play lanes (Release 6.6 / Wave 4)

**Status:** Pure-TS model + screen wiring + 148 new doctrine-anchored tests landed. The Conversation Gallery's section grouping is now a 10-lane "scrum board": each lane invites a specific kind of next move. Issue #30.

- **Why this card exists:** Stage 6.4 shipped a 6-section catalogue (`jump_in` / `needs_rebuttal` / `source_trail` / `hot_unresolved` / `easy_first_move` / `my_rooms`) but the lanes blurred together — `hot_unresolved` mixed active live disputes with stuck deep chains, and the catalogue did not surface evidence / definition / synthesis / branch-pressure as their own lanes. GAL-001 expands the catalogue to 10 lanes matching the kind of move a user wants to make, makes lane derivation deterministic (lifecycle > bucket > heat priority chain), and replaces the bucket chip row with a lane chip filter row.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` — replaces `GALLERY_SECTIONS` (6 entries) with `GALLERY_SECTION_DEFINITIONS` (10 frozen entries, each carrying `label` ≤ 64 chars / ≤ 8 tokens, `helperLine` ≤ 80 chars, `emptyCopy` ≤ 120 chars). Adds `GallerySectionDefinition` interface. Keeps `GALLERY_SECTIONS` as a one-release alias so the existing `seamlessConversationEntry.test.ts` import keeps compiling.
  - `src/features/debates/conversationGalleryModel.ts` — expands `ConversationGallerySection` union to 10 values: `my_rooms` / `needs_rebuttal` / `jump_in` / `source_trail` / `evidence_needed` / `definition_fights` / `logic_traps` / `tangents_branches` / `almost_synthesis` / `quiet_beginner_rooms`. Exports frozen `SECTION_ORDER`, re-exports `GALLERY_SECTION_DEFINITIONS`, and exports the previously-private `classifyCardToSection` so unit tests assert the priority chain directly. `GallerySectionGroup` gains a `helperLine` field. `classifyCardToSection` uses the documented 14-row priority chain (joined > no-rebuttal > 4 lifecycle priorities > 5 bucket priorities > overheated-heat fallback > 2 SW-002 entryOpportunity tie-breakers > quiet_beginner_rooms fallback).
  - `src/features/debates/ConversationGalleryScreen.tsx` — replaces `BucketChip` with `LaneChip`: single-select chip row keyed by `ConversationGallerySection`. "All lanes" chip resets the filter; tapping the active lane chip toggles back to "all". Each chip carries `accessibilityRole="button"`, `accessibilityState.selected`, an `accessibilityHint` populated from the lane helperLine, and a `hitSlop` lifting the effective tap target to ~48px (>= 44 per accessibility-targets). New `LaneSectionHeader` renders the lane label + helperLine above the card list. In single-lane filter mode the screen renders only that lane's cards (paginated). In all-lanes mode it groups the paginated cards via `groupGalleryCardsBySection` so each non-empty lane gets a section heading. Style names `bucketRowInner` / `sortRowInner` renamed to `laneRowContent` / `sortRowContent` to avoid an incidental "winner" substring on the plain-language source scan.
  - `__tests__/seamlessConversationEntry.test.ts` — updates the catalogue assertion to the 10-lane list. Rewrites the two affected routing assertions (`hot_now` → `jump_in`, `pedantic_plain + cold` → `quiet_beginner_rooms`). Adds 3 new routing assertions for `evidence_needed` / `definition_fights` / `almost_synthesis`.
  - `__tests__/galleryLaneDerivation.test.ts` — 63 new tests covering every row of the priority chain, cross-priority interactions (joined > lifecycle > bucket > heat), `groupGalleryCardsBySection` ordering / elision / one-card-one-lane invariants, `SECTION_ORDER` totality with an exhaustive-switch compile-time guard, back-compat assertions for the surviving Stage 6.4 routing rows + the documented `hot_unresolved` split, and purity / determinism (deep-equality on repeated calls, input not mutated, undefined-vs-null parity).
  - `__tests__/gallerySectionCopy.test.ts` — 29 new tests covering completeness (10 entries, one per union member, order matches SECTION_ORDER), length budgets, doctrine ban-list (verdict / popularity / person-attribution tokens forbidden; word-boundary scanning avoids false positives on routine English; `right` / `wrong` intentionally not banned because they are plain-language English with no verdict semantics in this catalogue), plain-language guard (no snake_case / no raw lane id leaks), heat-as-activity doctrine, accessibility metadata sanity, frozen-structure invariants.
  - `__tests__/galleryLaneFilter.test.tsx` — 56 new source-scan + contract tests following the existing `argumentReplySidecar.test.tsx` pattern. Asserts: lane chip row present with `lane-chip-` testID prefix; bucket chip row removed (no `bucket-chip-` testIDs, no `BUCKET_DEFINITIONS` reference, no `activeBucket` state); single-select state with chip toggle-back behaviour; accessibility metadata complete (role / state / hint / hitSlop); lane section rendering uses `groupGalleryCardsBySection` in all-lanes mode and `classifyCardToSection` in single-lane mode; observer-default entry preserved (GAL-002 / Stage 6.4 contract intact); no AI / Supabase / network imports; plain-language guard ban-list clean.
- **Behaviour change (documented):** the Stage 6.4 `hot_unresolved` lane is **retired**. Cards previously routed there now split: `hot_now` bucket and `overheated` heatLevel route to `jump_in`; `unresolved_deep_chain` bucket routes to `logic_traps`. The Stage 6.4 `easy_first_move` lane is **renamed** to `quiet_beginner_rooms`; classification rule unchanged. No production runtime code reads the retired strings — only tests + docs, all migrated.
- **Resolved design questions (operator-confirmed):**
  1. Bucket chip row vs lane chip row — the bucket-only chip filter is REMOVED. Lanes replace it. Buckets stay as internal classification on `ConversationGalleryCard.bucket` and feed lane derivation but are not user-selectable on the gallery UI.
  2. `SECTION_ORDER` placement of `my_rooms` — `my_rooms` is FIRST.
  3. `hot_unresolved` removal — ACCEPTED. Cards split between `jump_in` and `logic_traps` per the priority chain.
  4. Lane derivation file split — left in `conversationGalleryModel.ts` (file size ~1500 lines, well under any practical threshold and the lane logic is small + tightly coupled to the existing dedupe + sort helpers).
- **Doctrine encoded:** No verdict / popularity / person-attribution tokens in any authored string (verified by `gallerySectionCopy.test.ts` ban-list scan). Heat framed as activity / friction (`jump_in` helper: "Active back-and-forth — a fresh move lands cleanly."), never popularity / correctness. `logic_traps` describes move structure ("Same-axis pressure has repeated without new information."), not a verdict. `almost_synthesis` describes structural convergence, not correctness. Lane derivation reads only structural / activity / lifecycle descriptors — never popularity / engagement / virality / view counts / follower counts (doctrine §3).
- **Boundary enforcement:** `conversationGalleryModel.ts` lane derivation is pure / total / deterministic — no `Date.now` / `Math.random` / `fetch` / `anthropic` / `xai`. `ConversationGalleryScreen.tsx` source-scan refuses Supabase client, Anthropic SDK, xAI, raw fetch, XMLHttpRequest, `Date.now`, `Math.random`, `console.log`, `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`, `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` literals.

## SW-002 — Heat, momentum, trend without truth claims (Release 6.6 / Wave 2)

**Status:** Pure-TS deriver + 79 doctrine-anchored tests landed. Activity-model layer that future Gallery + mini-map cards (GAL-001 / GAL-002 / IX-002) consume read-only. No UI in this card.

All verdict-adjacent tokens (`winning / losing / dominant / losing ground / gaining ground / proven / disproven / verdict / validated / correct / incorrect / right / wrong / true / false`) ban-listed. Person-attribution tokens (`you / your / they / their / the user / the author / the poster / the participant`) ban-listed. Forbidden-imports scan refuses `buildPointLifecycleMap` / `buildMoveMetadataLedger` / `deriveAutoMetadataForMessage` / `gradeChallenge` / `gradeRepair` / `applyAntiAmplification` / `Date.now` / `Math.random` / `supabase` / `fetch` / `anthropic` / `xai` / `console.log` / `XMLHttpRequest` / secret literals in executable code (comments + string literals stripped before scan).

## ST-002 — Suggested reply flags per bubble card (Release 6.6 / Wave 2)

**Status:** Pure-TS deriver + SC-003 stub widening + 74 tests landed. The sidecar's `SuggestedNextMove` slot is now structurally population-ready; SC-003's builder behaviour is unchanged (still emits `suggestion: null` + `reason: 'st_002_not_yet_implemented'`). The render-side chip + integrator wiring are future cards.

- **Why this card exists:** SC-003 reserved a typed `SuggestedMoveStub = never` slot on the sidecar view-model so a future card could widen it to a real `SuggestedNextMove` union. ST-002 fills that slot with a pure-TS deriver that turns lifecycle (LIFE-001) + manual tag + auto-metadata (META-001) + evidence source-chain (EV-001) state into a small, ordered list of advisory suggested moves. Each suggestion carries a plain-language rationale assembled from RULE-003 helper lines (never freshly authored), an existing `QuickActionLabel` preset key, an optional SC-004 dock action, and a structural `sourceSignals[]` record for AN-003 diagnostics. Issue #13.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/arguments/suggestedMovesModel.ts` — pure TS. No React, no Supabase, no network, no AI. Exports `SuggestedMoveCode` (9-value union: `ask_source` / `ask_quote` / `narrow` / `concede` / `confirm` / `challenge_mechanism` / `challenge_scope` / `branch_tangent` / `synthesize`), `SuggestionSignal` (discriminated union covering source-chain / lifecycle / manual-tag / auto-metadata / 4 narrow signal kinds / `preset_gap`), `SuggestedMove` (`code` + `label` ≤ 24 chars + `rationale` ≤ 80 chars + `presetKey` + `dockAction` + `sourceSignals`), `SuggestionDerivationInput` (lifecycle / metadata / move-linkage / source-chain status / standing / depth / branch / tangent / `maxSuggestions`), `SuggestedNextMove = SuggestedMove`, plus `deriveSuggestedMoves(input)` (pure, total, deterministic; default `maxSuggestions = 3`), `buildRationale(signals)`, `_forbiddenSuggestionTokens()`. The three documented gap codes (`challenge_mechanism` → `challenge`, `challenge_scope` → `narrow`, `branch_tangent` → `branch`) route to existing presets and emit a `preset_gap` signal so AN-003 / PRESET-001 can track them.
  - `src/features/arguments/argumentReplySidecarModel.ts` — type-level widening only: `SuggestedMoveStub` changes from `never` to `SuggestedMove` (one new `import type`, one type alias change). No behaviour change in `buildSidecarViewModel(...)`. The SC-003 happy-path tests that pin `suggestion === null` continue to pass; the runtime tautology test that pins `SuggestedMoveStub | null` accepting `null` also continues to pass because the widening is purely additive.
  - `__tests__/suggestedMovesModel.test.ts` — 66 tests covering empty / null inputs (5), parameterized lifecycle-state primary coverage across all 19 `PointLifecycleState` values, parameterized manual-tag override across all 9 promotable tags + 1 deferred (`definition_issue`), parameterized auto-metadata refinement (6 promotions), parameterized source-chain override (4 statuses that fire + 2 that do not), preset mapping invariant (every `presetKey` is a member of `QuickActionLabel`), dock-action mapping invariant, exhaustive rationale ban-list scan (every signal kind × every code) against `_forbiddenSuggestionTokens()`, person-attribution scan against the COPY-001 token list (`you / your / they / their / the user / the author / the poster / the speaker / the participant / this person / this user`), snake_case scan on rationale + label, cap enforcement (rationale ≤ 80 / label ≤ 24 / array length ≤ `maxSuggestions`), gap-code routing (`challenge_mechanism` / `challenge_scope` / `branch_tangent` each pin their preset + dock + `preset_gap` signal), no-forced-gate contract (empty array is a valid output; no `onPress|onAction|dispatch|callback|handler` field name), determinism (deep-equality + stable signal order), standing-band ignored doctrine check, source-scan for engagement / amplification identifier reads (comment-stripped), forbidden-imports scan (`buildPointLifecycleMap` / `deriveAutoMetadataForMessage` / `gradeChallenge` / `gradeRepair` / `applyAntiAmplification` / `supabase` / `fetch` / `anthropic` / `xai` / `ArgumentComposer` / `react` / `react-native`), `ALL_SUGGESTED_MOVE_CODES` reachability coverage, and `SuggestedNextMove` type re-export round-trip.

- **Doctrine encoded:** Suggestions describe move shape — never the author (zero `you / your / they / their / the user / the author / the poster / the speaker / the participant / this person / this user` token in any rationale). Score never blocks posting — empty suggestion array is a valid output. No popularity / engagement / heat / virality input is consumed (source-scan enforces no identifier read of `engagement / amplification / likes / shares / followers / trending / viral`). No new presets — every `presetKey` is a pre-existing `QuickActionLabel`. No live AI — pure deterministic TS, same inputs → same outputs. The dock owns execution; ST-002 produces data only (no `onPress` / `onAction` / `dispatch` / `callback` / `handler` field). Rationale text comes from the RULE-003 helper-line vocabulary or is derived from existing plain-language phrases; nothing is freshly authored per call. `definition_issue` manual tag is documented as deferred (no `clarify`-shaped `SuggestedMoveCode` in v1).

## SC-003 — Sidecar as detail inspector (Release 6.6 / Wave 2)

**Status:** Pure-TS view-model + sidecar refactor + 81 tests landed. The sidecar is now the read-only detail inspector; SC-004's `TimelineNodeActionDock` remains the sole owner of the action palette.

- **Why this card exists:** Stage 6.2's `ArgumentReplySidecar` duplicated the action vocabulary (the `OTHER_ACTIONS` / `SELF_ACTIONS` arrays + `actionsRow`) that SC-004's dock already renders directly above it. SC-003 strips the sidecar back to the role its name promises — a detail inspector — and routes every label through RULE-003. The sidecar now explains the selected message in 6 fixed sections (`What this move says`, `Why it matters`, `What is unresolved`, `Where it sits`, `Suggested next move`, `Semantic flags`). Issue #11.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/arguments/argumentReplySidecarModel.ts` — pure-TS view-model + builder + `buildSidecarViewModel(input)`. No React, no Supabase, no network, no AI. Reads `getLifecycleUx` / `getManualTagUx` / `getAutoMetadataUx` from RULE-003. Reserves the ST-002 slot via `SuggestedMoveStub = never` so a later card can widen the union without breaking consumers.
  - `src/features/arguments/ArgumentReplySidecar.tsx` — refactored to consume a single `viewModel: SidecarViewModel` prop. Old action affordances (`OTHER_ACTIONS` / `SELF_ACTIONS` / `actionsRow` / `onAction` callback) removed. No body-edit affordance. No `<TextInput>` mounted. Only interactive is the Timeline-mode "Show details" toggle, which is purely presentational state.
  - `src/features/arguments/ArgumentGameSurface.tsx` — single call site updated to build the view-model from existing `lifecycleMap` + `metadataLedger` memos and pass it through.

  - `__tests__/argumentReplySidecar.test.tsx` — 13 source-scan + contract tests asserting the component has no SC-004 action references, no body-edit affordance, no `onAction` prop, only a `viewModel` prop, preserves the `argument-reply-sidecar` testID, exposes accessibility on the Show-details toggle (`accessibilityRole` + `accessibilityLabel` + `hitSlop`), and contains no router/navigation primitive.

No callback / dispatch field in the view-model. SC-003 ↔ SC-004 boundary test-enforced via two source scans (model + component). ST-002 contract reserved via `SuggestedMoveStub = never`.

## RULE-003 — Lifecycle-to-UX doctrine map (Release 6.6 / Wave 3)

**Status:** Pure-TS constants + readers + 31 tests landed. Render-ready map for SC-003 / ST-002 / GAL-002 / IX-002 consumers; no UI surface bound yet.

- **Why this card exists:** Single source of truth that maps every LIFE-001 point-lifecycle state (19), every META-001 manual tag (10), and every META-001 auto-derived metadata code (16) to a `{ label, helperLine, iconHint, allowedDockActions[] }` UX triple. The `label` field is READ through `getPointLifecyclePlainLabel` / `getManualTagPlainLabel` / `getAutoMetadataPlainLabel` at module-load time — never freshly authored — so a future rename in `PLAIN_LANGUAGE_COPY` cannot silently drift this surface. Consumers (SC-003 cluster headers, ST-002 suggested-move chips, GAL-002 gallery cards, IX-002 keyboard hint surface) read one map and stay doctrine-clean by construction. Issue #65.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/rulesUx/lifecycleUxMap.ts` — 3 frozen `Record<Union, Entry>` maps (19 + 10 + 16 = 45 entries), 24-value `IconHint` semantic vocabulary (verdict glyphs excluded), `DockAction` type alias re-using SC-004's `TimelineNodeActionDockActionCode`, and three total-lookup readers (`getLifecycleUx` / `getManualTagUx` / `getAutoMetadataUx`).
  - `__tests__/lifecycleUxMap.test.ts` — 31 tests covering coverage, label parity (anti-drift), ban-list scans against `_forbiddenLifecycleTokens()` + `_forbiddenMetadataTokens()` with word-boundary matching for the longer helper-line surface, snake_case + internal-code scans, person-attribution scan, heat/popularity/engagement scan, ≤ 80-char length cap, icon-hint validity + no-verdict-glyph check, action-vocabulary subset check + `expand_branch` / `mark_moved_on` / `mark_ignored` exclusion, reader reference-equality, cross-map label reuse for the truly shared `quote_requested` + `source_requested` codes, and `Object.isFrozen` invariants.
- **Doctrine encoded:** No verdict tokens in any label or helperLine. No person-attribution in any helperLine (side labels "Affirmative" / "Negative" are OK; "the author" / "you" / "they" are not). No truth / popularity / heat language. `allowedDockActions[]` is advisory only — SC-004's actor matrix (own-bubble / observer / etc.) still applies on top. `expand_branch` / `mark_moved_on` / `mark_ignored` intentionally never recommended.
- **No xAI, Anthropic, or X API calls; no Supabase writes; no service-role; no migration; no Edge Function change; no new dependency; no `.env*` touched; no hosting file touched.**
- **+31 tests / +1 suite** (3363 → 3394 tests passing-baseline-delta; 122 → 123 suites). The 5 pre-existing xAI / AI-bot corpus suites that fail in the baseline are unrelated to this card and remain operator-gated. Typecheck + lint clean. `skills:validate` clean.
- **No operator follow-up** — pure local change. No deploy step.

## COPY-001 — Plain-language label review pass + ban-list gap hardening (Release 6.6 / Wave 1 follow-up)

**Status:** Audit deliverable landed + optional ban-list hardening applied. Pure docs + ban-list arrays + new regression test — zero label change, zero behavior change.

Audit §5.1 + §8 record the carve-out.
  - `__tests__/copyReviewBanListGaps.test.ts` — new 7-test regression suite asserts each of `right`, `wrong`, `validated` is present in both ban-list helpers, that `hot` is NOT in either array (pins the doctrine §2 carve-out as a test invariant), and re-runs the per-label scan against the expanded ban-list to prove zero current labels in `PLAIN_LANGUAGE_COPY` trip the new tokens.
- **Label policy held:** zero entry in `PLAIN_LANGUAGE_COPY` changed. Audit found zero drifts; the hardening is purely additive — it catches future drift without forcing any current label rewrite or snapshot update. The 5 render-rules (R1 scope-strict positioning, R2 same-label dedup, R3 provenance suffix on cross-level reuse, R4 runner-status suppression in normal-user surfaces, R5 axis-vs-manual-tag dedup) are owned by consumer cards (SC-004 already implements R1+R2; ST-002 and RULE-003 are pending consumers).
